<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在使用工具时需要在推理深度与结构有效性之间取得平衡，现有方法要么直接复用原始示例输出效果有限，要么缺乏对历史执行经验的系统性利用。

Method: 提出CAST框架，将历史执行轨迹视为结构化案例，从中提取复杂度特征（用于估计最优推理策略）和失败模式（用于映射结构断裂点），设计细粒度奖励信号并实现自适应推理，通过强化学习使模型自主内化案例策略。

Result: 在BFCLv2和ToolBench上，执行准确率最高提升5.85个百分点，平均推理长度减少26%，有效降低了高影响的结构性错误。

Conclusion: 历史执行案例能够提供可复用的适应性知识，实现校准后的工具使用，平衡了推理深度与结构有效性。

Abstract: Tool use extends large language models beyond parametric knowledge, but reliable execution requires balancing appropriate reasoning depth with strict structural validity. We approach this problem from a case-based perspective to present CAST, a case-driven framework that treats historical execution trajectories as structured cases. Instead of reusing raw exemplar outputs, CAST extracts case-derived signals to identify complexity profiles for estimating optimal reasoning strategies, alongside failure profiles to map likely structural breakdowns. The framework translates this knowledge into a fine-grained reward design and adaptive reasoning, enabling the model to autonomously internalize case-based strategies during reinforcement learning. Experiments on BFCLv2 and ToolBench demonstrate that CAST improves both schema-faithful execution and task-level tool-use success while reducing unnecessary deliberation. The approach achieves up to 5.85 percentage points gain in overall execution accuracy and reduces average reasoning length by 26%, significantly mitigating high-impact structural errors. Ultimately, this demonstrates how historical execution cases can provide reusable adaptation knowledge for calibrated tool use.

### [97] [Dual-Dimensional Consistency: Balancing Budget and Quality in Adaptive Inference-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15100)
*Rongman Xu,Yifei Li,Tianzhe Zhao,Yanrui Wu,Bo Li,Hang Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出双维度一致性(DDC)框架，通过置信度加权贝叶斯协议和趋势感知分层剪枝，在推理时实现采样宽度与深度的统一优化，将token消耗降低10倍以上同时保持或提升推理准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推理时扩展策略在采样预算与推理质量之间存在权衡困境：宽度共识方法易强化幻觉，深度剪枝机制会过早截断复杂但有效的推理链。宽度和深度被当作正交目标分别优化，效率低下。

Method: 提出DDC统一框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 置信度加权贝叶斯协议(Confidence-Weighted Bayesian Protocol)，用于桥接路径质量与自适应终止；(2) 趋势感知分层剪枝(Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning)，用于将计算资源集中在高质量推理路径上，过滤幻觉并加速共识形成。

Result: 在五个基准测试上，DDC将token消耗降低超过10倍，同时在多种LLM上保持或超越了强基线的准确率。

Conclusion: DDC通过统一框架有效解决了推理时扩展中宽度与深度的权衡问题，实现了计算效率与推理质量的双重提升。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in reasoning. However, maximizing their potential through inference-time scaling faces challenges in trade-off between sampling budget and reasoning quality. Current strategies remain inefficient as they typically treat sampling width and depth as orthogonal objectives, where width consensus methods risk reinforcing hallucinations, while depth pruning mechanisms prematurely truncate complex yet valid reasoning chains. Therefore, we propose Dual-Dimensional Consistency (DDC), a unified framework that bridges path quality with adaptive termination. By coupling Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol with a Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning, our method ensures that computational resources are concentrated on high quality reasoning paths, filtering hallucinations while accelerating consensus. Evaluations across five benchmarks demonstrate that this approach reduces token consumption by over 10 times while maintaining or exceeding the accuracy of strong baselines across various LLMs.

</details>


### [98] [Why Neighborhoods Matter: Traversal Context and Provenance in Agentic GraphRAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15109)
*Riccardo Terrenzi,Maximilian von Zastrow,Serkan Ayvaz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 在Agentic GraphRAG中，引用的忠实性不仅取决于最终答案是否支持引用，还涉及整个图遍历轨迹、图结构以及已访问但未引用的实体。实验表明，被引证据通常是必要的，但仅靠引用并不足以保证答案的可靠性，未引用的遍历上下文和周围图结构也会影响答案准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过受控消融实验，对比隔离、移除和掩码处理已引用和未引用的图实体，分析这些操作对答案变化和准确性的影响。

Result: 被引证据被移除时答案显著变化且准确性下降，说明被引证据是必要的；但即使被引证据保留，未引用的遍历上下文和周围图结构也会影响答案准确性，说明仅凭被引证据不足以保证答案可靠。

Conclusion: Agentic GraphRAG中的引用评估应从传统的来源支持（source support）扩展到更广泛的检索轨迹溯源（provenance over the broader retrieval trajectory）。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation can improve factuality by grounding answers in external evidence, but Agentic GraphRAG complicates what it means for citations to be faithful. In these systems, an agent explores a knowledge graph before producing an answer and a small set of citations. We frame citation faithfulness as a trajectory-level problem: final citations should not only support the answer, but also account for the graph traversal, structure, and visited-but-uncited entities that may influence it. Through controlled ablation experiments, we compare the effects of isolating, removing, and masking cited and uncited graph entities. Our results show that cited evidence is often necessary, as removing it substantially changes answers and reduces accuracy. However, citations are not sufficient, because accurate answers can also depend on uncited traversal context and surrounding graph structure. These findings suggest that citation evaluation in Agentic GraphRAG should move beyond source support toward provenance over the broader retrieval trajectory.

### [99] [APWA: A Distributed Architecture for Parallelizable Agentic Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15132)
*Evan Rose,Tushin Mallick,Matthew D. Laws,Cristina Nita-Rotaru,Alina Oprea*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出APWA架构，一种分布式多智能体系统架构，用于高效处理高度可并行化的智能体工作负载，通过将工作流分解为非干扰性子问题实现并行执行，在复杂查询分解和任务扩展性上优于现有系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的自主多智能体系统在任务规模和复杂度增长时，面临推理、协调和计算扩展瓶颈，无法充分利用底层LLM中的并行计算和推理原语实现高吞吐量处理。

Method: APWA将工作流分解为无相互干扰的子问题，使用独立资源并行处理，无需跨通信；支持异构数据和多种并行处理模式，可适应广泛领域的任务。

Result: APWA能够动态将复杂查询分解为可并行化的工作流，在更大规模任务上表现出良好的扩展性，而现有系统在此类场景下完全失败。

Abstract: Autonomous multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in independently solving complex tasks in a wide breadth of application domains. However, these systems hit critical reasoning, coordination, and computational scaling bottlenecks as the size and complexity of their tasks grow. These limitations hinder multi-agent systems from achieving high-throughput processing for highly parallelizable tasks, despite the availability of parallel computing and reasoning primitives in the underlying LLMs. We introduce the Agent-Parallel Workload Architecture (APWA), a distributed multi-agent system architecture designed for the efficient processing of heavily parallelizable agentic workloads. APWA facilitates parallel execution by decomposing workflows into non-interfering subproblems that can be processed using independent resources without cross-communication. It supports heterogeneous data and parallel processing patterns, and it accommodates tasks from a wide breadth of domains. In our evaluation, we demonstrate that APWA can dynamically decompose complex queries into parallelizable workflows and scales on larger tasks in settings where prior systems fail completely.

### [100] [OpenDeepThink: Parallel Reasoning via Bradley--Terry Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15177)
*Shang Zhou,Wenhao Chai,Kaiyuan Liu,Huanzhi Mao,Qiuyang Mang,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OpenDeepThink是一种基于群体的测试时计算扩展框架，通过成对Bradley-Terry比较进行候选选择，在8轮LLM调用（约27分钟）内将Gemini 3.1 Pro的Codeforces Elo提升+405分，并在客观可验证领域表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时计算扩展主要通过延长单条推理轨迹来扩展深度，而扩展宽度（并行采样多个候选）面临选择瓶颈：在缺乏真实验证器的情况下，逐点LLM评判存在噪声和偏差，难以选出最佳候选。

Method: 提出OpenDeepThink框架：(1) LLM对随机配对的候选进行成对比较并生成自然语言批评；(2) 通过Bradley-Terry模型聚合投票生成全局排名；(3) 保留排名靠前的候选，对前四分之三的候选使用比较中产生的自然语言批评进行变异，丢弃后四分之一的候选。每代重复此过程。

Result: (1) Gemini 3.1 Pro的Codeforces Elo提升+405分（8轮，约27分钟）；(2) 框架可跨强弱模型迁移，无需重新调整；(3) 在多领域HLE基准上，增益集中在客观可验证领域，在主观领域则相反；(4) 发布了CF-73数据集（73个专家评级的Codeforces问题，含国际特级大师标注，本地评估与官方判定一致率达99%）。

Conclusion: 基于成对Bradley-Terry比较的群体选择方法能有效解决测试时计算扩展中的选择瓶颈，在客观可验证任务上提升显著，且具有良好的模型迁移性。

Abstract: Test-time compute scaling is a primary axis for improving LLM reasoning. Existing methods primarily scale depth by extending a single reasoning trace. Scaling breadth by sampling multiple candidates in parallel is straightforward, but introduces a selection bottleneck: choosing the best candidate without a ground-truth verifier, since pointwise LLM judging is noisy and biased. To address this, we introduce OpenDeepThink, a population-based test-time compute framework that selects via pairwise Bradley-Terry comparison. Each generation, the LLM judges random pairs of candidates and aggregates votes via Bradley-Terry into a global ranking; top-ranked candidates are preserved and the top three quarters are mutated using the natural-language critiques produced during comparison; the bottom quarter is discarded. OpenDeepThink raises Gemini 3.1 Pro's effective Codeforces Elo by +405 points in eight sequential LLM-call rounds (~27 minutes wall-clock). The pipeline transfers across weaker and stronger models without retuning, and on the multi-domain HLE benchmark, gains appear concentrated in objectively verifiable domains and reverse in subjective ones. We release CF-73, a curated set of 73 expert-rated Codeforces problems with International Grandmaster annotation and 99% local-evaluation agreement against the official verdict.

</details>

### [101] [Vision-Based Runtime Monitoring under Varying Specifications using Semantic Latent Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13923)
*Bardh Hoxha,Oliver Schön,Hideki Okamoto,Lars Lindemann,Georgios Fainekos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在部分可观测视觉数据下对过去时间信号时序逻辑(ptSTL)进行认证运行时监控的方法。通过引入“语义基”(semantic basis)概念，实现了无需针对每个公式重新训练的通用监控框架，并利用保形校准提供有限样本保证。在行人交叉路口和Waymo驾驶数据集上验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监控方法在部分可观测视觉环境下缺乏有限样本保证，且不同公式需要分别重新训练，效率低下。本文旨在设计一种可重用的监控接口，一旦训练和校准完成，就能认证目标片段中的任意公式，无需针对每个公式重新训练。

Method: 1) 提出“语义基”概念：由有限字典中时序原子的鲁棒性分数组成的向量，被证明是单调、1-Lipschitz可重用接口类中的最小预测目标。2) 任意公式通过解析树派生的确定性解码器求值。3) 单次保形校准即可认证整个公式片段，无需联合界。4) 引入滚动预测监控器，仅预测当前谓词值并在线重构时序历史，更容易学习但在长时域上保守性增加。

Result: 在行人交叉路口基准上，滚动监控器在短时域上获得更紧的认证界，而语义基监控器在长时域上紧度高达4倍。在真实Waymo驾驶数据上，两种监控器均经验性满足保形覆盖保证。

Conclusion: 语义基框架实现了可重用的ptSTL认证监控，有效平衡了学习难度与认证紧度，为安全关键视觉系统中的时序逻辑监控提供了理论保证和实用方案。

Abstract: We study certified runtime monitoring of past-time signal temporal logic (ptSTL) from visual observations under partial observability. The monitor must infer safety-relevant quantities from images and provide finite-sample guarantees, while being \emph{reusable}: once trained and calibrated, it should certify any formula in a target fragment without per-formula retraining. For fragments induced by a finite dictionary of temporal atoms, we prove that the \emph{semantic basis}, the vector of atom robustness scores, is the minimum prediction target within the class of monotone, 1-Lipschitz reusable interfaces: any formula is evaluated by a deterministic decoder derived from the parse tree, and a single conformal calibration pass certifies the entire fragment with no union bound. We also introduce a \emph{rolling prediction monitor} that predicts only current predicate values and reconstructs temporal history online; this is easier to learn but grows conservative at long horizons. On a pedestrian-crossroad benchmark, rolling achieves tighter certified bounds at short horizons while the semantic-basis monitor is up to 4-times tighter at long horizons. We validate the presented monitors on real-world Waymo driving data, where both monitors satisfy the conformal coverage guarantee empirically.

</details>


### [102] [Mechanistic Interpretability of EEG Foundation Models via Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13930)
*William Lehn-Schiøler,Magnus Ruud Kjær,Rahul Thapa,Magnus Guldberg Pedersen,Anton Storgaard Mosquera,Nick Williams,Radu Gatej,Tue Lehn-Schiøler,Sándor Beniczky,Sadasivan Puthusserypady,James Zou,Lars Kai Hansen*

TL;DR: 本文在三个不同架构的EEG基础模型（SleepFM、REVE、LaBraM）上应用TopK稀疏自编码器提取稀疏特征字典，通过临床分类体系（异常、年龄、性别、用药）基准测试单义性和纠缠度，并引入概念导向和目标vs离靶探针面积指标来量化导向选择性，发现选择可导向、编码但纠缠、未编码三种操作模式，暴露了"破坏球"干预和临床纠缠（如年龄-病理混淆）等表征失败，最终通过频谱解码器将潜在操作映射为生理可解释的频率特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在SleepFM、REVE和LaBraM三个架构上统一应用TopK稀疏自编码器提取稀疏特征；利用临床分类体系（异常、年龄、性别、用药）标注特征；提出基于字典健康审计的单超参数流程实现跨架构迁移；引入目标vs离靶探针面积指标量化概念导向选择性；通过频谱解码器将潜在干预映射到幅度谱。

Result: 概念导向存在三种操作模式：选择可导向、编码但纠缠、未编码；发现了"破坏球"干预（全局性能崩溃）和临床纠缠（如年龄-病理混淆无法解耦）；频谱解码器成功将干预映射为病理慢波抑制和α波段恢复等生理可解释信号。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了跨EEG基础模型架构的可解释性基准框架，揭示了当前模型存在的表征缺陷（纠缠和全局崩溃），并通过频谱映射建立了潜在空间操作与生理信号之间的可解释桥梁，为临床部署提供了信任基础。

Abstract: EEG foundation models achieve state-of-the-art clinical performance, yet the internal computations driving their predictions remain opaque: a barrier to clinical trust. We apply TopK Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) across three architecturally distinct EEG transformers: SleepFM, REVE, and LaBraM to extract sparse feature dictionaries from their embeddings. By grounding these features in a clinical taxonomy (abnormality, age, sex, and medication), we benchmark monosemanticity and entanglement across architectures. A single hyperparameter procedure, driven by an intrinsic dictionary health audit, transfers robustly across all three architectures. Via concept steering, we introduce a "target vs. off-target" probe area metric to quantify steering selectivity and reveal three operational regimes: selectively steerable, encoded but entangled, and non-encoded. This framework exposes critical representational failures: "wrecking-ball" interventions that collapse global model performance, and clinical entanglements, such as age-pathology confounding, where it is impossible to suppress one concept without corrupting the other. Finally, a spectral decoder maps these interventions back to the amplitude spectrum, translating latent manipulations into physiologically interpretable frequency signatures, such as pathological slow-wave suppression and $α$-band restoration.

### [103] [Rethinking Molecular OOD Generalization via Target-Aware Source Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13932)
*Zhuohao Lin,Kun Li,Jiameng Chen,Jiajun Yu,Duanhua Cao,Yizhen Zheng,Wenbin Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对分子性质预测中的极端分布外（OOD）泛化问题，提出了SCOPE-BENCH基准（基于理化描述符空间的聚类划分）和POMA框架（通过检索-组合-适配流程，利用强化学习策略自适应选择最优源子集，并在宏观拓扑和微观药效团两个尺度进行域自适应），实验表明现有3D分子模型在SCOPE-BENCH上预测误差平均扩大5.9倍，而POMA在不同骨干架构上平均提升6.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有scaffold-splitting协议无法阻止微观语义重叠，导致模型捷径学习并高估真实外推能力；传统域自适应方法在极端结构偏移下盲目对齐异构源库会引入拓扑噪声并引发负迁移。亟需更严格的OOD评估基准和更鲁棒的多源自适应框架。

Method: 提出SCOPE-BENCH基准，基于显式理化描述符空间进行聚类级划分；提出POMA框架，构建检索-组合-适配流水线：先识别与无标签目标结构接近的标记源支架作为代理目标，再利用强化学习策略从指数级候选池中自适应选择最优源子集，最后在宏观拓扑和微观药效团两个尺度进行双尺度域自适应。

Result: SOTA 3D分子模型在SCOPE-BENCH上预测误差最高达8.0倍，平均5.9倍；POMA在不同骨干架构上实现最高11.2%的MAE降低，平均相对提升6.2%。

Conclusion: 现有分子性质预测模型在极端OOD场景下的泛化能力被严重高估，而提出的POMA框架通过自适应多源选择和双尺度域自适应能有效缓解负迁移，显著提升极端结构偏移下的预测性能。

Abstract: Robust prediction of molecular properties under extreme out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios is a pivotal bottleneck in AI-driven drug discovery. Current scaffold-splitting protocols fail to obstruct microscopic semantic overlap, predisposing models to shortcut learning and overestimating their true extrapolation capability; meanwhile, conventional domain adaptation paradigms suffer under extreme structural shifts, as blindly aligning heterogeneous source libraries injects topological noise and triggers negative transfer. To address these two challenges, scaffold-cluster out-of-distribution performance evaluation benchmark (SCOPE-BENCH), a benchmark built on cluster-level partitioning in an explicit physicochemical descriptor space, is proposed alongside policy optimization for multi-source adaptation (POMA), a framework that formulates knowledge transfer as a retrieve-compose-adapt pipeline: labeled source scaffolds structurally close to the unlabeled target are first identified as proxy targets; a reinforcement learning policy then adaptively selects the optimal source subset from an exponentially large candidate pool; and dual-scale domain adaptation is finally performed at macroscopic topological and microscopic pharmacophore scales. Evaluations show that prediction errors of state-of-the-art 3D molecular models surge by up to 8.0x on SCOPE-BENCH with a mean of 5.9x, while POMA achieves up to an 11.2% reduction in mean absolute error with an average relative improvement of 6.2% across diverse backbone architectures. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Molecular-OOD-Code-73F6.

</details>


### [104] [Unsupervised learning of acquisition variability in structural connectomes via hybrid latent space modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13933)
*Gaurav Rudravaram,Lianrui Zuo,Karthik Ramadass,Elyssa McMaster,Jongyeon Yoon,Aravind R. Krishnan,Adam M. Saunders,Chenyu Gao,Nancy R. Newlin,Praitayini Kanakaraj,Lori L. Beason Held,Murat Bilgel,Laura A. Barquero,Micah DArchangel,Tin Q. Nguyen,Laurie B. Cutting,Derek Archer,Timothy J. Hohman,Daniel C. Moyer,Bennett A. Landman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无监督框架（Joint-VAE），通过架构退火（architectural annealing）替代手动容量调优，在dMRI结构连接组分析中自动将采集相关变异（扫描仪、协议差异）分离到离散潜变量中，而将生物变异保留在连续潜变量中。在N=7,416个连接组的数据集上，该方法在捕获采集变异方面优于VAE、PCA+k-means等基线方法（ARI=0.53, p<0.05）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: dMRI中不同站点、扫描仪和协议的采集差异引入变异性，干扰结构连接组分析。现有降维方法将变异建模为连续的，导致采集效应混入连续潜空间；而混合潜空间模型需手动容量调优以确保离散组件捕获目标变异，缺乏自动化机制。

Method: 提出Joint-VAE，通过在解码前对编码器输出进行架构退火（architectural annealing），自适应平衡离散与连续潜变量，无需手动调优。数据集包含N=7,416个结构连接组（2-102岁，13项研究，25种采集参数组合），对比标准VAE、PCA+k-means及仅通过损失函数退火的混合模型。

Result: 架构退火产生更强的站点学习效果（ARI=0.53, p<0.05），优于所有基线。Joint-VAE能够恢复与扫描仪和协议差异对齐的聚类结构。

Conclusion: 混合连续-离散潜空间结合架构退火，为dMRI中捕获采集变异性提供了有效的无监督机制，能够分离采集相关变异与生物变异。

Abstract: Acquisition differences across sites, scanners, and protocols in dMRI introduce variability that complicates structural connectome analysis. This motivates deep learning models that can represent high-dimensional connectomes in a low-dimensional space while explicitly separating acquisition-related effects from biological variation. Conventional dimensionality reduction methods model all variance as continuous, so acquisition effects often get absorbed into a continuous latent space. Recent hybrid latent-space models combine discrete and continuous components to address this, but typically require manual capacity tuning to ensure the discrete component captures the intended variability. We introduce an unsupervised framework that removes this manual tuning by architecturally annealing encoder outputs before decoding, allowing the model to adaptively balance discrete and continuous latent variables during training. To evaluate it, we curated a dataset of N=7,416 structural connectomes derived from dMRI, spanning ages 2 to 102 and 13 studies with 25 unique acquisition-parameter combinations. Of these, 5,900 are cognitively unimpaired, 877 have mild cognitive impairment (MCI), and 639 have Alzheimer's disease (AD). We compare against a standard VAE, PCA with k-means clustering, and hybrid models that anneal only through the loss function. Our architectural annealing produces stronger site learning (ARI=0.53, p<0.05) than these baselines. Results show that a hybrid continuous-discrete latent space, with architectural rather than loss-based annealing, provides a useful unsupervised mechanism for capturing acquisition variability in dMRI: by jointly modeling smooth and categorical structure, the Joint-VAE recovers clusters aligned with scanner and protocol differences.

### [105] [Beyond Mode-Seeking RL: Trajectory-Balance Post-Training for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13935)
*Saba Ahmadi,Prasanna Parthasarathi,Yufei Cui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TraFL方法，通过轨迹平衡目标解决扩散语言模型后训练中的轨迹锁定问题，在数学推理和代码生成任务上持续优于基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散语言模型的后训练方法大多采用奖励最大化目标，这会导致"轨迹锁定"问题：奖励驱动的更新将概率质量过度集中在少量去噪路径上，降低了重复采样时替代正确解的覆盖率。

Method: 提出TraFL（Trajectory Flow baLancing），采用轨迹平衡目标，将策略训练导向以冻结参考模型为锚点的奖励倾斜目标分布。通过扩散兼容的序列级替代目标和学习的提示相关归一化实现实用化。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成基准上，TraFL是唯一在所有基准长度设置下均优于基线模型的评估后训练方法，且收益随采样预算增加而持续。在Minerva Math和LiveCodeBench的各个难度级别上均保持领先。

Conclusion: TraFL有效解决了扩散语言模型后训练中的轨迹锁定问题，通过轨迹平衡目标实现了更鲁棒的奖励优化，并在多个任务上取得一致的性能提升。

Abstract: Diffusion language models are a promising alternative to autoregressive models, yet post-training methods for them largely adapt reward-maximizing objectives. We identify a central failure mode in this setting we call trajectory locking: sampled reward-driven updates over-concentrate probability mass onto a narrow set of denoising paths, reducing coverage of alternative correct solutions under repeated sampling. To address this, we propose TraFL (Trajectory Flow baLancing), a trajectory-balance objective that trains the policy toward a reward-tilted target distribution anchored to a frozen reference model. We make this practical for diffusion language models with a diffusion-compatible sequence-level surrogate and a learned prompt-dependent normalization. Across mathematical reasoning and code generation benchmarks, TraFL is the only evaluated post-training method that improves over the base model in every benchmark-length setting, with gains that persist as the sampling budget increases. The improvements transfer to held-out evaluations: TraFL stays above the base model on Minerva Math and is the strongest method on every LiveCodeBench difficulty split.

### [106] [Towards the Next Frontier of LLMs, Training on Private Data: A Cross-Domain Benchmark for Federated Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13936)

Conclusion: 联邦参数高效微调（Federated PEFT）是一种在隐私保护和监管合规约束下，利用分布式私有数据适配大语言模型的有效且高效的方法，为解锁高价值但不可共享的机构数据提供了实用路径。

Abstract: The recent success of large language models (LLMs) has been largely driven by vast public datasets. However, the next frontier for LLM development lies beyond public data. Much of the world's most valuable information is private, especially in highly regulated sectors such as healthcare and finance, where data include patient histories or customer communications. Unlocking this data could represent a major leap forward, enabling LLMs with deeper domain expertise and stronger real-world utility. Yet, these data cannot be shared because they are distributed across institutions and constrained by privacy, regulatory, and organizational barriers. Moreover, institutional datasets are typically non-independent and identically distributed (non-IID), differing across sites in population characteristics, data modalities, documentation patterns, and task-specific label distributions.
  In this paper, we demonstrate a practical approach to unlocking private and distributed institutional data for LLM adaptation through federated collaboration across data silos. Built on the Sherpa.ai Federated Learning platform, our framework enables nodes to jointly fine-tune a shared LLM without exchanging private data. We evaluate this approach through a cross-domain benchmark in healthcare and finance, using four closed-ended question answering and classification datasets: MedQA, MedMCQA, FPB, and FiQA-SA. We compare three parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) strategies-LoRA, QLoRA, and IA3-across pretrained backbones under non-IID settings reflecting institutional data heterogeneity. Our results show that federated fine-tuning performs close to centralized training and outperforms isolated single-institution learning. From a Green AI perspective, QLoRA and IA3 improve efficiency with limited accuracy degradation, supporting federated PEFT as a viable approach for adapting LLMs where data cannot be shared.

### [107] [EvolveMem:Self-Evolving Memory Architecture via AutoResearch for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13941)
*Jiaqi Liu,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EvolveMem提出了一种自我演化的记忆架构，不仅存储内容会更新，检索机制（评分函数、融合策略、答案生成策略）也会通过LLM驱动的诊断模块自动优化，在LoCoMo和MemBench上分别超越最强基线25.7%和18.9%，且演化出的配置具有跨基准迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体记忆系统在部署后检索基础设施（评分函数、融合策略、答案生成策略）是固定的，无法自适应演化，限制了跨会话长期记忆的效果。

Method: 提出EvolveMem架构，将完整检索配置暴露为结构化动作空间，由LLM驱动的诊断模块在每轮演化中读取失败日志、识别根因并提议配置调整；配备元分析器实现回归回滚和停滞探索的自动防护，形成闭环自我演化（AutoResearch过程）。

Result: 在LoCoMo上相对最强基线提升25.7%，相对最小基线提升78.0%；在MemBench上相对最强基线提升18.9%。演化出的配置跨基准测试呈现正向迁移，而非灾难性迁移。

Conclusion: 自我演化过程能够自主发现有效的检索策略，甚至包括原始动作空间中不存在的新配置维度，且捕获了普适的检索原则而非基准特定启发式。

Abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents that operate across multiple sessions, yet existing memory systems treat retrieval infrastructure as fixed: stored content evolves while scoring functions, fusion strategies, and answer-generation policies remain frozen at deployment. We argue that truly adaptive memory requires co-evolution at two levels: the stored knowledge and the retrieval mechanism that queries it. We present EvolveMem, a self-evolving memory architecture that exposes its full retrieval configuration as a structured action space optimized by an LLM-powered diagnosis module. In each evolution round, the module reads per-question failure logs, identifies root causes, and proposes targeted configuration adjustments; a guarded meta-analyzer applies them with automatic revert-on-regression and explore-on-stagnation safeguards. This closed-loop self-evolution realizes an AutoResearch process: the system autonomously conducts iterative research cycles on its own architecture, replacing manual configuration tuning. Starting from a minimal baseline, the process converges autonomously, discovering effective retrieval strategies including entirely new configuration dimensions not present in the original action space. On LoCoMo, EvolveMem outperforms the strongest baseline by 25.7% relative and achieves a 78.0% relative improvement over the minimal baseline. On MemBench, EvolveMem exceeds the strongest baseline by 18.9% relative. Evolved configurations transfer across benchmarks with positive rather than catastrophic transfer, indicating that the self-evolution process captures universal retrieval principles rather than benchmark-specific heuristics. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/SimpleMem.

### [108] [EMA: Efficient Model Adaptation for Learning-based Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13942)

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的系统缺乏对异构、长期运行和动态环境状态的适应支持，导致模型训练成本高、数据收集量大、系统性能下降和响应缓慢。

Method: 提出EMA系统，采用系统驱动、数据为中心的方法：(1) 引入状态转换器(State Transformers)将新环境输入状态对齐到先前相似状态，实现模型热启动适应；(2) 优先标注高效用数据，平衡训练与标注成本的权衡。

Result: 在8个代表性学习型系统上，EMA将适应成本（如GPU训练时间）降低14.9-42.4%，同时系统性能（如网络吞吐量）提升6.9-31.3%。

Conclusion: EMA作为首个模型自适应系统，以最小操作开销有效支持学习型系统适应动态环境，缓解了训练成本和数据标注两大关键部署挑战。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) is increasingly applied to optimize system performance in tasks such as resource management and network simulation. Unlike traditional ML tasks (e.g., image classification), networked systems often operate in heterogeneous, long-running, and dynamic environment states, where input conditions (e.g., network loads) and operational objectives can shift over time and across settings. Existing learning-based systems offer little support for adaptation, resulting in costly model training, extensive data collection, degraded system performance, and slow responsiveness.
  This paper presents EMA, the first model adaptation system supporting learning-based systems to adapt to evolving environments with minimal operational overhead. EMA takes a system-driven, data-centric approach that accommodates diverse system and model designs while addressing two key deployment challenges. First, it reduces expensive model training by introducing state transformers that align the input state of a new environment with previously similar states, allowing models to warm-start adaptation. Second, it addresses the often-overlooked yet costly process of data labeling--collecting ground truth for exploring and training on various system decisions--by prioritizing labeling high-utility data while balancing the tradeoff between training and labeling cost. Evaluations on eight representative learning-based systems show that EMA reduces adaptation costs (e.g., GPU training time) by 14.9-42.4% while improving system performance (e.g., network throughput) by 6.9-31.3%.

### [109] [A Unified Geometric Framework for Weighted Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13943)
*Raphael Vock,Edouard Duchesnay,Benoit Dufumier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过将加权InfoNCE目标解释为距离几何问题，揭示了对比学习中权重方案决定了几何可实现性：平衡SupCon退化为正则单纯形几何，类别不平衡导致SupCon出现非均匀类间相似度，而Soft SupCon保持正则单纯形；连续标签场景中，y-Aware CL因欧氏权重与球面潜相似度不匹配而无法达到熵最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对比学习旨在保留样本间的关系结构，但嵌入的几何特性尚未被充分理解。

Method: 将加权InfoNCE目标解释为距离几何问题，分析不同权重方案下的最优嵌入几何特性。

Result: 平衡SupCon退化为正则单纯形几何，类别不平衡导致SupCon出现非均匀类间相似度；Soft SupCon无论类别是否平衡均保持正则单纯形；y-Aware CL在连续标签场景中无法达到熵最优，除非标签位于超球面上。

Conclusion: 权重方案的选择决定了对比学习是否几何可实现、退化或不一致，为设计对比学习目标提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Contrastive learning (CL) aims to preserve relational structure between samples by learning representations that reflect a similarity graph. Yet, the geometry of the resulting embeddings remains poorly understood. Here we show that weighted InfoNCE objectives can be interpreted as Distance Geometry Problems, where the weighting scheme specifies the target geometry to be realized by the representation. This viewpoint yields exact characterizations of the optimal embeddings for several supervised and weakly supervised objectives. In supervised classification, both SupCon and Soft SupCon (a dense relaxation of it where pairs from distinct classes have small non-zero similarity) collapse samples within each class to a single prototype. However, while balanced SupCon recovers the classical regular simplex geometry, class imbalance breaks this symmetry: SupCon induces non-uniform inter-class similarities depending on class sizes, whereas Soft SupCon preserves a regular simplex geometry regardless of class imbalance. In continuous-label settings, our framework reveals a different failure mode: y-Aware CL generally cannot attain its entropic optimum unless the labels lie on a hypersphere, exposing a mismatch between Euclidean label weights and spherical latent similarity. By contrast, geometrically consistent choices such as Euclidean-Euclidean weighting or X-CLR admit unique optimal embeddings. Our results show that the choice of weighting scheme determines whether contrastive learning is geometrically realizable, degenerate, or inconsistent, providing a principled framework for designing contrastive objectives.

Abstract: Autonomous language-model agents are increasingly evaluated on long-horizon tool-use tasks, but existing benchmarks rarely capture the complexity and nuance of real scientific work. To address this gap, we introduce Collider-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating whether LLM agents can reproduce experimental analyses from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) using only public papers and open scientific software. Such analyses are often difficult to reproduce because the public toolchain only approximates the software used internally by the experimental collaborations, while the published papers inevitably omit implementation details needed for a faithful reconstruction. Agents must therefore rely on physical reasoning, domain knowledge, and trial-and-error to fill these gaps. Each task requires the agent to turn a published analysis into an executable simulation-and-selection pipeline and submit predicted collision event yields in specified signal regions. These predictions are evaluated with standard histogram metrics that provide continuous fidelity scores without a hand-written rubric. We also report the computational cost incurred by each agent per task. Finally, we evaluate the codebase and full session trace using an LLM judge to catch qualitative failure modes such as fabrications, hallucinations and duplications. We release an initial set of tasks drawn from LHC searches, together with a containerized sandbox and event simulation tools. We evaluate across a capability ladder of general purpose coding agents. Our results show that on average no agent reliably beats the physicist-in-the-loop solution.

### [111] [WarmPrior: Straightening Flow-Matching Policies with Temporal Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13959)
*Sinjae Kang,Chanyoung Kim,Kaixin Wang,Li Zhao,Kimin Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出WarmPrior，一种基于近期动作历史构建的简单时间接地先验分布，替代扩散/流匹配模型中标准的高斯源分布，能一致提升机器人操控任务的成功率，并改善强化学习的样本效率与最终性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出在基于扩散和流匹配的生成式机器人控制策略中，源分布（source distribution）是一个重要且尚未充分探索的设计维度，标准高斯分布并非最优。

Method: 提出WarmPrior：利用可获取的近期动作历史构建一个时间接地的简单先验分布，替代标准高斯分布作为生成模型的源分布。

Result: WarmPrior一致提升机器人操控任务的成功率；生成的路径更直，类似于Rectified Flow中最优传输耦合的效果；在基于先验空间的强化学习中同时改善样本效率和最终性能。

Abstract: Generative policies based on diffusion and flow matching have become a dominant paradigm for visuomotor robotic control. We show that replacing the standard Gaussian source distribution with WarmPrior, a simple temporally grounded prior constructed from readily available recent action history, consistently improves success rates on robotic manipulation tasks. We trace this gain to markedly straighter probability paths, echoing the effect of optimal-transport couplings in Rectified Flow. Beyond standard behavior cloning, WarmPrior also reshapes the exploration distribution in prior-space reinforcement learning, improving both sample efficiency and final performance. Collectively, these results identify the source distribution as an important and underexplored design axis in generative robot control.

Method: 1) 仅使用先验分布生成的合成数据预训练；2) 引入测试时计算扩展（test-time compute scaling），通过TabPFN-3-Plus (Thinking) API利用额外计算提升性能；3) 减少KV缓存和行分块（row-chunking）技术实现单卡H100扩展到100万行；4) 针对不同任务训练专门检查点（如TabPFN-TS-3用于时序）。

Abstract: Tabular data underpins most high-value prediction problems in science and industry, and TabPFN has driven the foundation model revolution for this modality. Pretrained exclusively on synthetic data from our prior, TabPFN-3 dramatically pushes the frontier of tabular prediction and brings substantial gains on time series, relational, and tabular-text data.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出NeTMY，一种无摊销的坐标神经场，与可微NV前向模型耦合；采用退火位置编码、多尺度优化、稀疏/门控机制和谱保真度损失函数。同时将标量/相干前向近似替换为张量功率求和偶极算子。

Abstract: Inverse problems in scientific sensing are often solved with either hand-designed regularizers or supervised networks trained on simulated labels, yet both can fail when the forward model is nonlinear, spectrally coupled, and physically delicate. We study this issue for noise sensing based on nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond, where a quantum sensor measures magnetic-noise spectra generated by sparse spin sources. We show that replacing a common scalar/coherent forward approximation with a tensor power-summed dipolar operator changes the inverse landscape and exposes a center-collapse failure mode in free-density optimization. We propose NeTMY, an amortization-free coordinate neural field coupled to the differentiable NV forward model, with annealed positional encoding, multiscale optimization, sparsity/gating, and spectrum-fidelity losses. Across sparse synthetic reconstructions generated by the corrected operator, NeTMY achieves the best localization and distributional metrics in the tested benchmark. Mechanism experiments show that NeTMY does not directly execute the raw density-space gradient; its parameterization smooths and redistributes updates, mitigating the center-collapse pathology. These results position NV quantum sensing as a useful testbed for physics-faithful neural inverse problems.

### [115] [HodgeCover: Higher-Order Topological Coverage Drives Compression of Sparse Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13997)
*Tao Zhong,Dongzhe Zheng,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了稀疏MoE层中现有无训练压缩方法的根本性障碍：三个两两兼容的专家可能形成不可约的合并环（即调和核）。通过Hodge分解将问题形式化，并提出了HodgeCover算法，在激进压缩场景下达到最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无训练MoE压缩方法均基于成对专家兼容性评分，但存在结构性盲区：三个两两兼容的专家可能构成不可约的循环（调和核），导致任何成对评分方法都无法判断三元组是否可联合合并。作者试图从数学上刻画并解决这一障碍。

Method: 1) 将障碍形式化为2-复形上的单纯拉普拉斯调和核，其中顶点为专家、边携带KL合并障碍、面携带三元组障碍；2) 通过Hodge分解将边障碍信号分解，精确分离出调和核；3) 提出HodgeCover算法，贪心覆盖调和关键边和三元组关键三角形；4) 提出混合变体，将HodgeCover与现成的权重剪枝结合。

Result: 在三个开源稀疏MoE模型上进行激进专家压缩实验，HodgeCover在专家压缩维度与SOTA无监督基线持平，在混合压缩维度（专家压缩+权重剪枝）的激进压缩前沿上领先，并在所有四个Hodge分量上实现了独特的质量保持平衡。

Conclusion: 揭示MoE结构的调和核能从根本上改变压缩器的性能格局，特别是在最关键的激进压缩场景下，哪些压缩器胜出会发生转变。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) layers route tokens through a handful of experts, and learning-free compression of these layers reduces inference cost without retraining. A subtle obstruction blocks every existing compressor in this family: three experts can each be pairwise compatible yet form an irreducible cycle when merged together, so any score that ranks experts on pairwise signals is structurally blind to which triples are jointly mergeable. We show the obstruction is a precise mathematical object, the harmonic kernel of the simplicial Laplacian on a 2-complex whose vertices are experts, whose edges carry KL merge barriers, and whose faces carry triplet barriers; Hodge-decomposing the edge-barrier signal isolates the kernel exactly. We turn the diagnostic into a selection objective: HodgeCover greedily covers the harmonic-critical edges and triplet-critical triangles, and a hybrid variant of HodgeCover pairs it with off-the-shelf weight pruning on survivors. On three open-weight Sparse MoE backbones under aggressive expert reduction, HodgeCover matches state-of-the-art learning-free baselines on the expert-reduction axis, leads on the aggressive-compression frontier of the hybrid axis, and uniquely balances retained mass across all four Hodge components. These results show that exposing the harmonic kernel of a learned MoE structure changes which compressor wins at the regime that matters most.

### [116] [Support Before Frequency in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13999)
*Adrian Müller,Antoine Gonon,Zebang Shen,Ya-Ping Hsieh,Niao He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解离散扩散模型的去噪目标如何组织学习过程，特别是模型如何从数据分布中恢复不同层次的信息。

Method: 理论证明了在小噪声（最终去噪步骤）条件下，单token反向编辑分解为领先尺度（数据支持）和精细系数（频率信息）；并通过实验验证（掩码语言扩散模型+合成正则语言任务）。

Result: 支持定位先于支持内频率排序出现；均匀扩散与吸收扩散在速率分离上符合理论预测。均匀扩散呈现三分性（有效性提升/保持/恶化），吸收扩散主要集中于有效性提升。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are increasingly competitive for language modeling, yet it remains unclear how their denoising objectives organize learning. Although these objectives target the full data distribution, we show that the exact reverse process induces a hierarchy between coarse support information and finer frequency information. For uniform and absorbing (a.k.a. masking) diffusion, we prove that, in the small-noise regime of the final denoising steps, each single-token reverse edit decomposes into a leading scale, determined by whether it moves toward the data support (e.g., grammatically valid sentences), and a finer coefficient, determining relative probabilities within the same scale. Thus, recovering validity structure only requires learning the correct order of magnitude of reverse probabilities, whereas recovering data frequencies requires coefficient-level estimation. The separation is mechanism-dependent: uniform diffusion exhibits a trichotomy into validity-improving, validity-preserving, and validity-worsening edits, while absorbing diffusion places its leading-order mass on validity-improving moves. Experiments on a masked language diffusion model and synthetic regular-language tasks support these predictions: support-localization emerges earlier than within-support frequency ranking, and the contrast between uniform and absorbing diffusion matches the predicted rate separation. Together, our results suggest that discrete diffusion models learn data support before data frequencies.

### [118] [Policy Optimization in Hybrid Discrete-Continuous Action Spaces via Mixed Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14297)
*Matias Alvo,Daniel Russo,Yash Kanoria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出混合策略优化（HPO）方法，用于解决混合离散-连续动作空间的强化学习问题。HPO通过混合梯度估计器（结合路径梯度和得分函数梯度）在平滑处反向传播模拟器梯度，保持无偏性，并可将动作不连续问题重构为混合形式。实验表明HPO在库存控制和切换线性二次调节器问题上显著优于PPO，且性能差距随连续动作维度增大而扩大。此外，混合梯度的交叉项在接近离散最优响应时可忽略，从而支持近似解耦更新并降低方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型无关策略梯度方法（如使用得分函数估计器）在高维连续动作空间中面临严重的信用分配问题，导致梯度质量差；而可微模拟器反向传播方法在面对离散动作或非光滑动力学时会产生有偏或无效梯度。因此需要一种能在混合离散-连续动作空间中保持梯度无偏且高效的方法。

Method: 提出混合策略优化（HPO），其核心是混合梯度估计器：在动力学平滑处通过模拟器反向传播路径梯度，在非平滑或离散处使用得分函数梯度，并保持整体估计的无偏性。此外，通过将动作不连续问题重构为混合形式扩展适用范围。

Result: 在库存控制和切换线性二次调节器问题上，HPO显著优于PPO，且性能差距随连续动作维度增加而扩大。同时，理论分析表明混合梯度的交叉项在接近离散最优响应时可忽略，支持近似解耦更新并降低最优性附近的方差。

Conclusion: HPO有效结合了路径梯度与得分函数梯度的优势，为混合离散-连续动作空间的强化学习提供了一种无偏、高效且可扩展的解决方案，尤其在高维连续动作场景下优势显著。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning in hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces, such as settings where the discrete component selects a regime (or index) and the continuous component optimizes within it -- a structure common in robotics, control, and operations problems. Standard model-free policy gradient methods rely on score-function (SF) estimators and suffer from severe credit-assignment issues in high-dimensional settings, leading to poor gradient quality. On the other hand, differentiable simulation largely sidesteps these issues by backpropagating through a simulator, but the presence of discrete actions or non-smooth dynamics yields biased or uninformative gradients. To address this, we propose Hybrid Policy Optimization (HPO), which backpropagates through the simulator wherever smoothness permits, using a mixed gradient estimator that combines pathwise and SF gradients while maintaining unbiasedness. We also show how problems with action discontinuities can be reformulated in hybrid form, further broadening its applicability. Empirically, HPO substantially outperforms PPO on inventory control and switched linear-quadratic regulator problems, with performance gaps increasing as the continuous action dimension grows. Finally, we characterize the structure of the mixed gradient, showing that its cross term -- which captures how continuous actions influence future discrete decisions -- becomes negligible near a discrete best response, thereby enabling approximate decentralized updates of the continuous and discrete components and reducing variance near optimality. All resources are available at github.com/MatiasAlvo/hybrid-rl.

</details>


### [119] [R2R2: Robust Representation for Intensive Experience Reuse via Redundancy Reduction in Self-Predictive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14026)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数据稀缺的真实机器人等强化学习场景中，高数据复用率（高UTD比率）虽然提升了样本效率，但会导致过拟合。现有工作主要关注评论家偏差，而自预测学习（SPL）在高UTD比率下表示层的不稳定性尚未被充分探索。

Method: 提出R2R2（Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction）正则化方法。理论上发现标准零中心化与SPL的谱特性存在冲突，据此设计了非中心化目标。在SPL原生算法TD7上验证，并将SPL模块集成到原本缺乏SPL的SOTA方法SimbaV2中，形成SimbaV2-SPL。

Result: 在11个连续控制任务上，UTD比率为20时，R2R2使TD7提升约22%，并在SimbaV2-SPL基础上带来额外增益，SimbaV2-SPL自身已建立了新的SOTA。

Conclusion: R2R2能有效缓解高UTD比率下SPL的表示层过拟合问题，且与现有先进方法正交，可作为通用正则化手段进一步提升性能。

Abstract: For reinforcement learning in data-scarce domains like real-world robotics, intensive data reuse enhances efficiency but induces overfitting. While prior works focus on critic bias, representation-level instability in Self-Predictive Learning (SPL) under high Update-to-Data (UTD) regimes remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method within SPL. We theoretically identify that standard zero-centering conflicts with SPL's spectral properties and design a non-centered objective accordingly. We verify R2R2 on SPL-native algorithms like TD7. Furthermore, to demonstrate its orthogonality to prior advancements, we extend the state-of-the-art SimbaV2, which originally lacks SPL, by integrating a tailored SPL module, termed SimbaV2-SPL. Experiments across 11 continuous control tasks confirm that R2R2 effectively mitigates overfitting; specifically, at a UTD ratio of 20, it improves TD7 by ~22% and provides additional gains on top of SimbaV2-SPL, which itself establishes a new state-of-the-art. The code can be found at: https://github.com/songsang7/R2R2

</details>

To incorporate prior knowledge and compliance requirements, we further introduce the Branching Structure Constraints (BSC) framework, which enables decision makers to encode domain knowledge and constraints directly into the model. This optimization-based approach discovers a hidden underlying pattern in datasets, when it exists, by identifying an optimal rule that maximizes coverage while minimizing the false positive rate due to misclassification. Our computational experiments show that OPDT discovers a pattern with optimality guarantees on moderately sized datasets within reasonable runtime.

### [121] [Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention: Learning When to Write by Predicting Future Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14037)
*Gergely Szilvasy,Manuel Faysse,Maria Lomeli,Matthijs Douze,Pierre-Emmanuel Mazaré,Loïc Cabannes,Wen-tau Yih,Hervé Jégou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV)，一种通过轻量级效用预测器动态剪枝KV缓存的方法，可在不影响性能的情况下将KV缓存大小减少3-10倍，并揭示出可用于指导混合注意力架构设计的结构化稀疏模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在测试时计算和智能体范式的驱动下，语言模型处理的序列越来越长，而Transformer架构中KV缓存的内存占用和带宽成为高效文本生成的主要瓶颈。

Method: SP-KV方法包含一个轻量级效用预测器，对每个键值对进行评分；通过局部窗口保留最近的KV对，而较旧的KV对仅在预测效用超过阈值时才写入缓存并用于全局注意力。模型与效用预测器通过下一个token预测损失进行端到端联合训练。

Result: SP-KV实现动态稀疏化，可将KV缓存大小减少3-10倍，长序列压缩率更高；在内存使用和解码速度上显著提升，验证损失和下游任务性能几乎没有下降。

Conclusion: SP-KV不仅是一种有效的KV缓存缩减机制，还揭示了层和注意力头特定的结构稀疏模式，可用于指导混合局部-全局注意力架构的设计。

Abstract: Under modern test-time compute and agentic paradigms, language models process ever-longer sequences. Efficient text generation with transformer architectures is increasingly constrained by the Key-Value cache memory footprint and bandwidth. To address this limitation, we introduce Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV), a mechanism designed to predict future KV utility in order to reduce the size of the long-term KV cache. This strategy operates at a fine granularity: a lightweight utility predictor scores each key-value pair, and while recent KVs are always available via a local window, older pairs are written in the cache and used in global attention only if their predicted utility surpasses a given threshold. The LLM and the utility predictor are trained jointly end-to-end exclusively through next-token prediction loss, and are adapted from pretrained LLM checkpoints.
  Rather than enforcing a fixed compression ratio, SP-KV performs dynamic sparsification: the mechanism adapts to the input and typically reduces the KV cache size by a factor of $3$ to $10\times$, longer sequences often being more compressible. This leads to vast improvements in memory usage and decoding speed, with little to no degradation of validation loss nor performance on a broad set of downstream tasks. Beyond serving as an effective KV-cache reduction mechanism, our method reveals structured layer- and head-specific sparsity patterns that we can use to guide the design of hybrid local-global attention architectures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对EM离散化导致的损失偏差进行理论分析，并设计一种无偏且免二阶导数的训练框架。

Abstract: Deep learning methods based on backward stochastic differential equations (BSDEs) have emerged as competitive alternatives to physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) for solving high-dimensional partial differential equations (PDEs). By leveraging probabilistic representations, BSDE approaches can avoid the curse of dimensionality and often admit second-order-free training objectives that do not require explicit Hessian evaluations. It has recently been established that the commonly used Euler-Maruyama (EM) time discretization induces an intrinsic bias in BSDE training losses. While high-order schemes such as Heun can fully eliminate this bias, such schemes re-introduce second-order spatial derivatives and incur substantial computational overhead. In this work, we provide a principled analysis of EM-induced loss bias and propose an unbiased, second-order-free training framework that preserves the computational advantages of BSDE methods. Our code is available at https://github.com/seojaemin22/Un-EM-BSDE.

### [123] [Reliability-Gated Source Anchoring for Continual Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14063)
*Vikash Singh,Debargha Ganguly,Weicong Chen,Sabyasachi Sahoo,Sreehari Sankar,Biyao Zhang,Mohsen Harir,Shouren Wang,Osama Zafar,Christian Gagné,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对持续测试时自适应（CTTA）中源模型在严重分布偏移下失效的"盲锚定"问题，提出RMemSafe方法，通过基于归一化预测熵的可靠性门控机制，动态减弱源锚定约束，在源模型不可靠时退化为无源备用损失，在CCC-Hard等极端场景下显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于源锚定的CTTA方法在源模型严重退化（如CCC-Hard上ResNet-50仅1.3%准确率）时仍保持相同锚定强度，导致性能崩溃，这种"盲锚定"失败模式亟需解决。

Method: 提出RMemSafe，作为ROID的扩展，引入可靠性门控机制：利用冻结源模型的归一化预测熵，当熵值接近均匀分布（源后验趋于均匀）时，关闭门控，消除源锚定和一致性滤波，将目标函数退化为无源备用损失（ROID基础损失+边缘校准）。

Result: 在9个匹配分割的持续损坏单元中，8个取得最低错误率；在所有9个单元中均为最佳重置方法；相比ROID+ASR，ResNet-50上提升1.05pp，ViT-B/16上提升0.48pp；源退化扫描中性能下降斜率仅为ROID+ASR的1/1.13，符合优雅退化预期。

Conclusion: 熵门控能有效检测高熵的源模型崩溃，而非低熵但错误自信的情况；该方法在源模型可靠性急剧下降时仍能保持稳健的自适应性能。

Abstract: Continual test-time adaptation (CTTA) updates a pretrained model online on an unlabeled, non-stationary stream while anchoring it to a frozen source checkpoint. This anchor is useful only when the source remains reliable. On CCC-Hard, however, a ResNet-50 source falls to approximately $1.3\%$ top-$1$ accuracy, while existing source-anchored CTTA methods continue applying the same anchor strength. We call this failure mode blind anchoring and propose RMemSafe, a reliability-gated extension of ROID that uses the frozen source's normalized predictive entropy to attenuate all explicit source-coupled uses in the objective. When the source posterior approaches uniformity, the gate closes: the source anchor and agreement filter vanish, and the objective reduces to a source-agnostic fallback comprising ROID's base losses plus marginal calibration. Combined with ASR, RMemSafe achieves the lowest error on $8$ of $9$ matched-split continual-corruption cells and is the best reset-based method on all $9$, improving ROID+ASR by $1.05$~pp on ResNet-50 and $0.48$~pp on ViT-B/16. A controlled source-degradation sweep shows a $1.13{\times}$ shallower harm slope than ROID+ASR, consistent with the graceful-decay prediction. The entropy gate detects high-entropy source collapse, not confidently wrong low-entropy sources; this scope is explicitly evaluated and discussed.

### [124] [In-Context Learning for Data-Driven Censored Inventory Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14840)
*Sohom Mukherjee,Anh-Duy Pham,Richard Pibernik,Yunbei Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合离线生成模型与在线决策的库存控制方法ICGPS，通过在潜在需求的学习补全上采取oracle行动，解决了传统参数化汤普森采样在先验不匹配下的脆弱性和离线插值方法无法迁移到在线学习的问题。理论上建立了贝叶斯遗憾边界，实践中使用ChronosFlow实现了快速且与审查一致的采样，实验表明该方法匹配正确设定的TS，优于基线方法，并对先验不匹配和分布偏移具有鲁棒性。

Method: 提出In-Context Generative Posterior Sampling (ICGPS)，利用离线元训练的生成模型，通过上下文自回归生成在线部署。理论框架将贝叶斯遗憾分解为理想TS基准的遗憾加上部署惩罚项。实践中结合ChronosFlow，使用冻结时间序列transformer骨干与可训练的条件归一化流头部。

Abstract: We study inventory control with decision-dependent censoring, focusing on the censored or repeated newsvendor (R-NV), where each order quantity determines whether demand is fully observed or censored by sales. Existing approaches based on parametric Thompson sampling (TS) can be brittle under prior mismatch, while offline imputation methods need not transfer to online learning. Motivated by the predictive view of decision making, we combine these ideas by taking oracle actions on learned completions of latent demand. We propose in-context generative posterior sampling (ICGPS), which uses modern generative models that are meta-trained offline and deployed online by in-context autoregressive generation. Theoretically, we show that the Bayesian regret of ICGPS with a learned completion kernel is bounded by the Bayesian regret of a TS benchmark with the ideal completion kernel plus a deployment penalty scaling as $\sqrt{T}$ times the square root of the completion mismatch. This yields a plug-in template for operational problems with known TS regret bounds. For R-NV, we derive sublinear Bayesian regret by reducing censored feedback to bandit convex optimization feedback. We also show that, under reasonable coverage and stability assumptions, the online completion mismatch is controlled by the offline censored predictive mismatch, so offline predictive quality transfers to online performance. Practically, we instantiate ICGPS with ChronosFlow, which combines a frozen time-series transformer backbone with a trainable conditional normalizing-flow head for fast censoring-consistent sampling. In benchmark experiments, ChronosFlow-ICGPS matches correctly specified TS, outperforms myopic and UCB-style baselines, and is robust to prior mismatch and distribution shift. ChronosFlow-ICGPS also performs well for the real-world SuperStore dataset, especially under heavy censoring.

### [126] [SurF: A Generative Model for Multivariate Irregular Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14069)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (i) 利用时间重标定理（TRT）构建可学习双射，将事件序列映射为i.i.d.单位速率指数噪声；(ii) 提出三种高效累积强度函数参数化方案，支持长序列扩展；(iii) 采用基于Transformer的编码器实现多数据集预训练。

Abstract: Irregularly sampled multivariate event streams remain a stubbornly difficult modality for generative modeling: tokenization-based approaches break down when inter-event intervals vary by orders of magnitude, and neural temporal point processes are bottlenecked by window-level numerical quadrature. We (i) propose SurF, a generative model that uses the Time Rescaling Theorem (TRT) as a learnable bijection between event sequences and i.i.d.\ unit-rate exponential noise, enabling a single model to be trained across heterogeneous event-stream datasets; (ii) three efficient parameterizations of the cumulative intensity that scale to long sequences; and (iii) a Transformer-based encoder for multi-dataset pretraining. On six real-world benchmarks, SurF achieves the best reported time RMSE on Earthquake, Retweet, and Taobao, and is within trial-level noise of the strongest specialist on the remaining three. Under a strict leave-one-out protocol, the held-out checkpoint beats every classical and neural-autoregressive baseline on 5/6 datasets and beats every baseline on Amazon and Earthquake, an initial step toward foundation models over asynchronous event streams.

Abstract: Learning of continuous exponential family distributions with unbounded support remains an important area of research for both theory and applications in high-dimensional statistics. However, theoretical understanding of the statistical properties of score matching is still lacking. In this work, we provide a non-asymptotic sample complexity analysis for learning the structure of exponential families of polynomials with score matching. The derived sample bounds show a polynomial dependence on the model dimension. These bounds are the first of its kind, as all prior work has shown only asymptotic bounds on the sample complexity.

</details>


### [128] [AttnGen: Attention-Guided Saliency Learning for Interpretable Genomic Sequence Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14073)
*Rayhaneh Shabani Nia,Ali Karkehabadi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AttnGen是一个注意力引导的训练框架，通过在训练过程中逐步抑制低贡献核苷酸位置，将可解释性直接嵌入优化过程。在demo_human_or_worm基准测试中，AttnGen在200核苷酸序列二分类任务上达到96.73%验证准确率，优于CNN基线（95.83%），同时表现出更快的收敛速度和更好的训练稳定性。扰动分析表明，去除高重要性核苷酸会使准确率从96.9%降至接近随机水平，说明模型依赖少量信息性位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络在基因组序列分类中表现优异，但将其预测与生物学上有意义的序列模式关联起来仍然具有挑战性。现有方法缺乏将可解释性直接融入训练过程的手段。

Method: 提出AttnGen框架：利用注意力机制计算核苷酸级重要性分数，在训练过程中逐步抑制低贡献位置，迫使模型聚焦于紧凑的信息区域。

Result: 在demo_human_or_worm基准上，AttnGen达到96.73%验证准确率（CNN基线95.83%），收敛更快且训练更稳定。去除高重要性核苷酸后，准确率从96.9%降至接近随机水平。10-20%的掩码率提供最佳性能-可解释性权衡。

Conclusion: 注意力引导的掩码不仅提升了分类性能，还重塑了模型在序列位置上分配重要性的方式。该方法虽针对短基因组序列设计，但可能扩展到更复杂的可解释序列建模场景。

Abstract: Deep neural networks have achieved strong performance in genomic sequence classification; however, relating their predictions to biologically meaningful sequence patterns remains challenging. In this work, we present AttnGen, an attention-guided training framework that embeds interpretability directly into the optimization process. AttnGen computes nucleotide-level importance scores using an attention mechanism and progressively suppresses low-contribution positions during training. This encourages the model to focus its predictions on a compact set of informative regions while reducing reliance on noisy sequence elements. We evaluate AttnGen on the standardized demo_human_or_worm benchmark, a binary classification task over 200-nucleotide sequences. With moderate masking, AttnGen achieves a validation accuracy of 96.73%, outperforming a conventional CNN baseline with 95.83% accuracy, while also exhibiting faster convergence and improved training stability. To assess whether the learned importance scores reflect functionally relevant signal, we conduct perturbation-based analysis by removing high-saliency nucleotides. This causes accuracy to drop from 96.9% to near chance level on a 3,000-sequence evaluation set, indicating that the model relies on a relatively small subset of informative positions. Our analysis shows that masking 10--20% of positions provides the most favorable trade-off between predictive performance and interpretability. These results suggest that attention-guided masking not only improves classification performance but also reshapes how models distribute importance across sequence positions. Although this study focuses on short genomic sequences, the proposed approach may extend to more complex interpretable sequence modeling settings.

### [129] [How to Scale Mixture-of-Experts: From muP to the Maximally Scale-Stable Parameterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14200)
*Leena Chennuru Vankadara,Moritz Haas,Luke Hayward,Sebastian Bordt,Alessandro Breccia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了混合专家模型（MoE）在宽度、专家宽度、专家数量和稀疏性等超参数下的缩放规律，发现现有最大更新参数化（μP）存在缩放不稳定问题，并提出了最大尺度稳定参数化（MSSP），通过动力学平均场理论（DMFT）验证其能实现学习率迁移和随规模单调提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前MoE架构在大模型中广泛使用，但缺乏超参数如何随网络宽度、专家宽度、专家数量和深度等维度缩放的理论理解，导致训练稳定性和最优性能无法得到保证。

Method: 针对三种缩放机制（协同缩放、共缩放、完全比例缩放），分别建立动力学平均场理论（DMFT）描述MoE的训练动力学。在DMFT框架下推导满足最大更新（μ）所有必要条件的SGD和Adam唯一定参化，然后基于最大尺度稳定原则推导最大尺度稳定参数化（MSSP）。

Result: μP不能可靠地实现随规模的单调提升或鲁棒的学习率迁移，原因是聚合动力学中存在尺度依赖的可观测变量。MSSP能鲁棒地恢复学习率迁移和随规模的单调提升，且通过独立的DMFT分析表征了其极限动力学。

Conclusion: 结合已有的深度缩放理论，给出了MoE架构在宽度、深度、专家宽度和专家数量上的完整缩放处方。

Abstract: Recent frontier large language models predominantly rely on Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures. Despite empirical progress, there is still no principled understanding of how hyperparameters should scale with network width $N$, expert width $N_e$, number of experts $M$, sparsity $K$, and depth $L$ to ensure both stability and optimal performance at scale. We take a principled step toward resolving this gap by analyzing three different scaling regimes: (I) co-scaling $N\asymp N_e$, (II) co-scaling $N\asymp M\asymp K$, and (III) full proportional scaling of $N, N_e, M$, and $K$. For each regime, we develop a novel Dynamical Mean Field Theory (DMFT) description of the limiting training dynamics of MoEs that provides a formal foundation for our analysis. Within this framework, we derive the unique parameterization for SGD and Adam satisfying all maximal-update ($μ$) desiderata. We then show that the resulting $μ$P prescription does not reliably induce monotonic improvement with scale or robust learning-rate transfer. We trace these pathologies to scale-dependent observables in the aggregation dynamics, which motivates a refined set of desiderata that we term maximal scale stability. Guided by this principle, we derive a Maximally Scale-Stable Parameterization (MSSP) for both SGD and Adam in all three scaling regimes, and characterize the corresponding limiting dynamics - qualitatively distinct from the $μ$P limit - through a separate DMFT analysis. Experiments verify that MSSP robustly recovers learning rate transfer and monotonic improvement with scale across regimes. Combined with existing depth-scaling theory, these results provide a complete scaling prescription for MoE architectures as a function of width, depth, expert width, and number of experts.

</details>


### [130] [Fair and Calibrated Toxicity Detection with Robust Training and Abstention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14074)
*Mokshit Surana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出毒害分类公平性需从排序、校准和弃权三个维度综合评估。实验发现：训练干预仅转移而非消除偏差，后处理机制继承训练失败模式，且弃权本身对不同身份组不公平。论证了公平性评估必须采用多轴框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的毒害分类公平性研究往往只关注单一维度（如排序或校准），忽略了不同公平性维度之间的相互影响，以及训练阶段干预与后处理安全机制之间的依赖关系。作者希望建立一个综合多轴的公平性评估框架。

Method: 对比三种训练方法（ERM、实例级重加权、Group DRO）结合三种后处理方法（温度缩放、基于置信度的弃权、每身份阈值优化），使用子组AUC、BPSN/BNSP AUC、误差差距和子组期望校准误差（ECE）等指标进行评估，并采用bootstrap置信区间（n=1000）。

Result: (1) 校准差异是隐藏的公平性违规，ERM聚合校准近乎完美(0.013)但各身份子组校准差(+0.029至+0.134)；(2) 重加权ERM提升排序但校准公平性差距恶化高达+0.232，DRO消除校准差异但全局校准变差(ECE 0.118)；(3) 温度缩放因校准非均匀而失效，置信度弃权在ERM下有效但在DRO下风险-覆盖曲线上升；(4) 弃权本身不公平，对背景内容帮助远大于身份提及内容。

Conclusion: SRAI公平性需要多轴评估框架：仅在聚合排序上表现不同的方法，在决定实际危害的失败模式上可能截然不同。

Abstract: Fairness in toxicity classification involves three integrated axes: ranking, calibration, and abstention. Training-time interventions and post-hoc safety mechanisms cannot be evaluated independently because the former determines the efficacy of the latter. We compare Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM), instance-level reweighting, and Group DRO across these axes, combined with temperature scaling, confidence-based abstention, and per-identity threshold optimization. Evaluation uses subgroup AUC, BPSN/BNSP AUC, error gaps, and per-subgroup Expected Calibration Error (ECE) with bootstrap CIs ($n = 1000$).
  We report four findings. (1) Calibration disparity is a hidden fairness violation. ERM has near-perfect aggregate calibration ($0.013$) but is significantly miscalibrated across all identity subgroups ($+0.029$ to $+0.134$). (2) Training interventions reshape rather than eliminate disparity. Reweighted ERM improves ranking (BPSN AUC $+0.06$ to $+0.12$) but worsens the calibration-fairness gap by up to $+0.232$. Group DRO eliminates calibration disparity but only by becoming uniformly miscalibrated globally (ECE $0.118$). (3) Post-hoc methods inherit training failure modes. Temperature scaling fails because miscalibration is non-uniform. Confidence-based abstention works under ERM but breaks under DRO, where the risk-coverage curve rises with deferral. (4) Abstention itself is unfair. Confidence-based deferral helps background content far more than identity-mentioning content. We argue that SRAI fairness requires a multi-axis framework: methods that differ only in aggregate ranking can differ sharply in failure modes that determine real-world harm.

### [131] [TILT: Target-induced loss tilting under covariate shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14280)
*Kakei Yamamoto,Martin J. Wainwright*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出TILT方法，通过分解源域预测器为f+b，在源域拟合f+b同时在目标域惩罚b，实现无监督域适应。理论证明该目标侧惩罚隐式实现相对重要性加权，且估计量b*_f有界。给出有限样本超额风险不等式和稀疏ReLU网络的端到端保证。实验表明TILT优于源域训练、精确重要性加权和相对密度比基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决协变量偏移下的无监督域适应问题，现有方法如重要性加权存在方差大、支持不重叠时失效等局限，需要一种更稳定且具有理论保证的方法。

Method: 将源域预测器分解为f+b，在带标签源域数据上拟合f+b，同时在无标签目标域数据上惩罚辅助分量b，最终将f作为目标域预测器。该方法在总体水平上隐式实现相对重要性加权，且估计量b*_f被局部化到当前误差并保持一致有界。

Result: 给出了总体水平的理论分析，证明了有限样本下的超额风险oracle不等式以及稀疏ReLU网络的端到端保证。在受控回归问题和偏移CIFAR-100蒸馏任务上，TILT优于源域训练、精确重要性加权和相对密度比基线，且对正则化参数具有稳定依赖。

Conclusion: TILT通过目标侧惩罚隐式实现重要性加权，解决了传统方法在支持不重叠等场景下的不稳定问题，提供了完整的理论保障并在实验中验证了有效性。

Abstract: We introduce and analyze Target-Induced Loss Tilting (TILT) for unsupervised domain adaptation under covariate shift. It is based on a novel objective function that decomposes the source predictor as $f+b$, fits $f+b$ on labeled source data while simultaneously penalizing the auxiliary component $b$ on unlabeled target inputs. The resulting fit $f$ is deployed as the final target predictor. At the population level, we show that this target-side penalty implicitly induces relative importance weighting at the population level, but in terms of an estimand $b^*_f$ that is self-localized to the current error, and remains uniformly bounded for any source-target pair (even those with disjoint supports). We prove a general finite-sample oracle inequality on the excess risk, and use it to give an end-to-end guarantee for training with sparse ReLU networks. Experiments on controlled regression problems and shifted CIFAR-100 distillation show that TILT improves target-domain performance over source-only training, exact importance weighting, and relative density-ratio baselines, with a stable dependence on the regularization parameter.

### [132] [Rethinking Layer Relevance in Large Language Models Beyond Cosine Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14075)
*Cristian Hinostroza,Rodrigo Toro Icarte,Christ Devia,Andres Carvallo De Ferari,Eugenio Herrera-Berg,Denis Parra,Jorge F Silva*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs内部机制的可解释性研究对开发更可解释和优化的架构至关重要，但现有广泛使用的余弦相似度指标可能无法准确反映层的重要性。

Method: 通过理论分析证明余弦相似度在极端情况下可与实际层重要性完全脱节；同时在多种LLM上进行实证实验，比较余弦相似度与实际层移除后性能下降的相关性。

Result: 理论分析表明层可以具有任意低的余弦相似度但仍然是模型性能的关键；实证结果证实余弦相似度与实际性能下降之间的相关性通常较弱或中等，导致对Transformer内部机制的错误解读。

Conclusion: 余弦相似度不适合评估层相关性，应改用实际移除层后的准确率下降作为更准确的度量，尽管计算成本更高，但能为剪枝策略和轻量模型提供更可靠的依据。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have revolutionized natural language processing. Understanding their internal mechanisms is crucial for developing more interpretable and optimized architectures. Mechanistic interpretability has led to the development of various methods for assessing layer relevance, with cosine similarity being a widely used tool in the field. On this work, we demonstrate that cosine similarity is a poor proxy for the actual performance degradation caused by layer removal. Our theoretical analysis shows that a layer can exhibit an arbitrarily low cosine similarity score while still being crucial to the model's performance. On the other hand, empirical evidence from a range of LLMs confirms that the correlation between cosine similarity and actual performance degradation is often weak or moderate, leading to misleading interpretations of a transformer's internal mechanisms. We propose a more robust metric for assessing layer relevance: the actual drop in model accuracy resulting from the removal of a layer. Even though it is a computationally costly metric, this approach offers a more accurate picture of layer importance, allowing for more informed pruning strategies and lightweight models. Our findings have significant implications for the development of interpretable LLMs and highlight the need to move beyond cosine similarity in assessing layer relevance.

Abstract: Domain adaptation faces a fundamental paradox in the cold-start regime. When target data is scarce, statistical methods fail to distinguish relevant source domains from irrelevant ones, which often leads to negative transfer. In this paper, we address this challenge by leveraging expert textual descriptions of the target domain, a resource that is often available but overlooked. We propose a probabilistic framework that translates these semantic descriptions into a choice model, namely a Language-Induced Prior (LIP), that learns the preferences from a pretrained Large Language Model (LLM). The LIP is then integrated into an Expectation-Maximization algorithm to identify source relevance. Methodologically, this framework is compatible with any parametric model where a likelihood is available. It allows the LIP to guide the selection of sources when target signals are weak, while gradually refining these choices as samples accumulate. Theoretically, we prove that the estimator roughly matches an oracle cold-start MSE under a correct prior, while remaining asymptotically consistent regardless of the quality of the LIP. Empirically, we validated the framework on a descriptive (Gaussian estimation), a predictive (C-MAPSS dataset), and a prescriptive task (MuJoCo hopper).

Answering clinically meaningful questions over FHIR requires agents to perform multi-step reasoning, filtering, and aggregation across multiple resource types. Prior work shows that even tool-augmented LLM agents (retrieval, code execution, multi-turn planning) often select the wrong resources or violate traversal constraints. We study this problem in the context of FHIR-AgentBench, a benchmark for realistic question answering over real-world hospital data, and frame reasoning on FHIR as a sequential decision-making problem over a queryable structured graph. We implement a multi-turn CodeAct agent and post-train it with reinforcement learning using a custom harness and tools. A LLM Judge provides execution-grounded rewards. Compared to prompt-based, closed-model baselines, RL post-training improves performance while enforcing data-integrity constraints. Empirically, our approach improves answer correctness from 50% (o4-mini) to 77% on FHIR-AgentBench using a smaller and cheaper Qwen3-8B model. We present an end-to-end post-training pipeline (environment building, harness construction, model training and custom evaluation) that reliably improves multi-turn reasoning over structured clinical graphs.

### [136] [Nearest-Neighbor Radii under Dependent Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14343)

Abstract: Nearest-neighbor methods are fundamental to classical and modern machine learning, yet their geometric properties are typically analyzed under independent sampling. In this paper, we study the nearest-neighbor radii under dependent sampling. We consider strong mixing dependent observations and ask whether dependence changes the scale of nearest-neighbor neighborhoods. We establish distribution-free almost sure convergence under polynomial mixing and sharp non-asymptotic moment bounds under geometric mixing. The moment bounds depend on the local intrinsic dimension rather than the ambient dimension, making the results applicable to high-dimensional data concentrated near lower-dimensional manifolds. Synthetic experiments and real-world time-series benchmarks support the theory, showing that nearest-neighbor geometry remains informative under dependence sampling.

### [138] [Fast Rates for Inverse Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14599)
*Andreas Schlaginhaufen,Maryam Kamgarpour*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文建立了熵正则化最小-最大逆强化学习（Min-Max-IRL）的结构性和统计性结果，证明了在总体层面和确定性动力学下的经验层面，最大似然估计（MLE）与Min-Max-IRL等价；利用伪自协方差性质，证明了轨迹级KL散度和Hessian范数下的平方参数误差以快速率$\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$衰减，且适用于模型误设定和无需探索假设的场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为熵正则化Min-Max-IRL建立严谨的结构性和统计性理论，解决其在连续状态-动作空间、模型误设定及无探索假设下的理论保证缺失问题。

Result: 1) MLE与Min-Max-IRL在总体层面等价，在确定性动力学下经验层面等价；2) 轨迹级KL散度和Hessian范数下平方参数误差以$\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$快速衰减；3) 奖励可辨识性结果推广至一般Borel空间；4) 获得软最优值函数关于奖励参数导数的全新结果。

Conclusion: 熵正则化Min-Max-IRL在连续状态-动作空间的有限时域MDP中具有坚实的理论和统计基础，能实现快速收敛，且对模型误设定具有鲁棒性，无需探索假设。

Abstract: We establish novel structural and statistical results for entropy-regularized min-max inverse reinforcement learning (Min-Max-IRL) with linear reward classes in finite-horizon MDPs with Borel state and action spaces. On the structural side, we show that maximum likelihood estimation (MLE) and Min-Max-IRL are equivalent at the population level, and at the empirical level under deterministic dynamics. On the statistical side, exploiting pseudo-self-concordance of the Min-Max-IRL loss, we prove that both the trajectory-level KL divergence and the squared parameter error in the Hessian norm decay at the fast rate $\mathcal{O}(n^{-1})$, where $n$ is the number of expert trajectories. Our guarantees apply under misspecification and require no exploration assumptions. We further extend reward-identifiability results to general Borel spaces and derive novel results on the derivatives of the soft-optimal value function with respect to reward parameters.

### [139] [A Systematic Evaluation of Imbalance Handling Methods in Biomedical Binary Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14147)

The evaluation encompassed three public biomedical datasets: MIMIC-III (tabular), ADE-Corpus-V2 (text), and MURA (image), spanning three common biomedical data modalities. To assess varying model complexity, we employed a range of architectures, from classical logistic regression and random forest to deep neural networks, including multilayer perceptron (MLP), BiLSTM, BERT, DenseNet, and DINOv2.
  Results: For simpler models such as logistic regression on tabular data, IHMs yielded no significant advantage over the RAW baseline, aligning with prior findings. However, clear benefits were observed for more complex models and unstructured data: (a) ROS and RW consistently enhanced the performance of powerful models; (b) direct F1-score optimization demonstrated utility primarily for unstructured text and image data; and (c) RUS and SMOTE consistently degraded performance and are therefore not recommended.

Abstract: While generative models have shown promise in pediatric sleep analysis, the latent structure of their multimodal embeddings remains poorly understood. ### [141] [A Mutual Information Lower Bound for Multimodal Regression Active Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14917)
*Leonardo Ferreira Guilhoto,Akshat Kaushal,Paris Perdikaris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对连续回归中主动学习在预测分布多峰时难以分离认知不确定性的问题，提出Two-Index框架分离认知与偶然不确定性，并推导MI-LB采集函数，在多模态基准上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续回归的主动学习采集函数（如方差、BALD）无法有效处理预测分布多峰情况：方差无法捕捉模态间的分歧，BALD等基于信息论的指标设计用于离散输出，不适用于连续回归。

Method: 提出Two-Index框架（一个随机索引表示模型假设，另一个表示假设内随机性），通过熵分解将信息采集目标对应为输出与模型索引间的互信息。针对连续输出下该互信息难计算的问题，推导出MI-LB（互信息下界）采集函数，用于混合密度网络集成。

Result: 在多模态系统基准上，MI-LB匹配或超越所有基线方法，并且是唯一一致表现良好的方法；几何和Fisher基线仅当输入空间已编码多模态时才有效，否则失效。

Conclusion: Two-Index框架为连续回归的认知不确定性分离提供了理论基础，MI-LB作为实用采集函数在多模态主动学习任务中具有一致优势。

Abstract: Active learning for continuous regression has lacked an acquisition function that targets epistemic uncertainty when the predictive distribution is multimodal: variance misses modal disagreement, and information-theoretic targets like BALD are designed for discrete outputs. We introduce a Two-Index framework that makes this separation explicit: one stochastic index selects among competing model hypotheses (epistemic source), while a second governs within-hypothesis randomness (aleatoric source). An entropy decomposition within the framework identifies the mutual information between the output and the epistemic index as a principled acquisition objective, and we prove this quantity vanishes as the model is trained on growing datasets, confirming that it captures exactly the uncertainty data can resolve. Because this mutual information is intractable for continuous outputs, we derive the Mutual Information Lower Bound (MI-LB) acquisition function, a closed-form approximation for Mixture Density Network ensembles. On benchmarks featuring multimodal systems, MI-LB matches or beats every baseline evaluated and is the only method to do so consistently -- geometric and Fisher-based baselines compete only when the input space already encodes the multimodality, and collapse otherwise.

### [142] [CSI-JEPA: Towards Foundation Representations for Ubiquitous Sensing with Minimal Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14171)
*Xuanhao Luo,Zhizhen Li,Yuchen Liu*

Method: CSI-JEPA采用自监督预测表示学习：1）将CSI时域-子载波二维幅度窗口进行令牌化；2）提出信道变化感知掩码策略，优先从局部时域和子载波域变化强烈的区域采样预测目标；3）预测可见上下文对应的掩码区域潜在特征。预训练后冻结编码器作为主干，为下游任务添加轻量级任务适配器。

Abstract: Channel state information (CSI) provides a widely available sensing modality for human and environment perception, but existing CSI sensing models usually rely on task-specific supervised training and require substantial labeled data for each task, device, user, or environment. This limits their scalability in practical deployments where unlabeled CSI is abundant but labeled data is costly to collect. In this paper, we present CSI-JEPA, a self-supervised predictive representation learning framework for label-efficient, multi-task Wi-Fi sensing. CSI-JEPA learns reusable temporal-spectral representations from unlabeled CSI samples by predicting latent features of masked channel regions from visible context. To better match the physical structure of CSI, CSI-JEPA tokenizes channel-response amplitude windows along the time and subcarrier dimensions. It then introduces a channel variation-aware masking strategy that samples predictive targets from regions with stronger local temporal and subcarrier-domain variations. After pretraining, the encoder is frozen and used as a backbone, with lightweight task-specific adapters added for downstream sensing tasks. We evaluate CSI-JEPA on seven real-world Wi-Fi sensing tasks spanning diverse objectives and deployment settings. The results show that CSI-JEPA improves downstream sensing performance over competitive baselines, achieving up to 10.64 percentage points mean accuracy gain over state-of-the-art supervised Transformer and matched-budget label savings of up to 98.0%.

### [143] [InfoSFT: Learn More and Forget Less with Information-Aware Token Weighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14967)

TL;DR: InfoSFT提出了一种基于信息量的加权方案，通过聚焦中等置信度token来改进监督微调，避免对低似然样本过拟合，同时保持模型原有能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准SFT对所有样本均匀拟合，包括那些在基模型下似然较低的样本，导致模型过度拟合特定样本而非学习目标行为，且因策略偏移过大而损害已有能力。现有过滤、降权等方法虽能缓解问题，但会抑制基模型尚未学习的新颖行为。

Method: InfoSFT是一种基于信息论原理的加权方案，为SFT目标函数中的每个token分配权重，聚焦于信息量最大、中等置信度的token——既不过于熟悉也不过于不稳定。该方法只需对标准token-wise损失函数进行一行代码修改。

Result: 在数学、代码和思维链任务上，使用多种模型家族，InfoSFT在泛化性能上显著优于标准SFT和基于似然加权的基线方法，同时更好地保留了模型原有的能力。

Conclusion: InfoSFT通过简单的一行代码修改，即可在保持计算效率的同时，有效提升SFT的泛化能力和模型稳定性。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) provides the standard approach for teaching LLMs new behaviors from offline expert demonstrations. However, standard SFT uniformly fits all samples -- including those with low likelihood under the base model -- which can disproportionately drive training updates toward overfitting specific samples rather than learning the target behavior. Moreover, adapting to these unlikely samples induces substantial policy shifts that degrade prior capabilities. Existing methods mitigate this by filtering, regenerating, or down-weighting low-likelihood data. In doing so, they often suppress precisely the novel behaviors the base model has yet to learn.
  We propose InfoSFT, a principled weighting scheme for the SFT objective that concentrates learning signals on maximally informative, medium-confidence tokens -- those neither overly familiar to the base model nor too unlikely to cause instability. Requiring only a one-line modification to the standard token-wise loss, InfoSFT demonstrably improves generalization over vanilla SFT and likelihood-weighted baselines across math, code, and chain-of-thought tasks with diverse model families, while better preserving pre-existing capabilities.

### [144] [LLMs Know When They Know, but Do Not Act on It: A Metacognitive Harness for Test-time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14186)
*Qi Cao,Yufan Wang,Peijia Qin,Shuhao Zhang,Pengtao Xie*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽能产生自我监控信号（如置信度估计），但这些信号通常被孤立地测量或引出，而未用于控制推理过程。受Nelson-Narens认知心理学理论启发，研究者希望将模型已有的元认知能力转化为有效的测试时控制机制。

Method: 提出元认知控制框架，分离监控与推理：模型先报告预求解FOK信号，求解后报告JOL信号；控制接口基于这些信号决定是否信任当前解、是否用元认知反馈重试、或是否将多次尝试传给最终聚合器。

Result: 在文本、代码和多模态推理基准上，固定Claude Sonnet-4.6基模型无参数更新即提升准确率从48.3到56.9，在HLE-Verified、LiveCodeBench v6和R-Bench-V三个主要评估设置上超过最强排行榜条目。
