### [260] [PI-SONet: A Physics-Informed Symplectic Operator Network for Real-Time Optimal Control of Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14332)
*Alan John Varghese,Shanqing Liu,Paula Chen,Yaochen Zhu,Jérôme Darbon,George Em Karniadakis*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: PI-SONet是一个结构保持的算子学习框架，通过将高维最优控制问题分解为辅助空间中的可解右端问题和辛算子，实现单一训练模型在亚秒级内泛化至新问题实例，相比基线方法获得高达10,000倍加速，为解决高维非线性最优控制问题提供了可复用的实时替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有最优控制求解器受限于维度诅咒，且每个新问题设置都需要完全重新运行，无法满足实时控制高维多智能体系统的实际需求。

Method: 提出PI-SONet框架，将参数化最优控制问题族及其Pontryagin最大原理系统分解为潜在右端空间求解器与条件辛算子两部分，在计算高效的辅助空间中生成可解的Hamilton轨迹，再变换回物理空间。

Result: 单一训练算子即可近似PMP解映射，内在地保持Hamilton结构，并能泛化至未见问题配置；在新问题上实现亚秒级推理，相比代表性基线方法获得高达10,000倍加速。

Conclusion: 结构保持的神经算子为高维最优控制提供了通向可复用、实时替代求解器的实用路径。

Abstract: Many real-life applications involve controlling high-dimensional multi-agent systems in real-time. Existing optimal control solvers often suffer from the curse-of-dimensionality and require complete rerunning for each new problem setting. We target nonconvex, nonlinear problems in 100s of dimensions by introducing PI-SONet (Physics-Informed Symplectic Operator Network), a structure-preserving operator learning framework for solving parameterized families of optimal control problems and their Pontraygin Maximum Principle (PMP) systems. PI-SONet combines a latent right-space solver with a conditional symplectic operator to produce tractable Hamiltonian trajectories in a computationally efficient auxiliary space and transform them back to physical space. This decomposition yields a \textit{single} trained operator that approximates the PMP solution map, inherently preserves Hamiltonian structure, and generalizes across unseen problem configurations. Unlike existing methods, which are fundamentally single-instance solvers, PI-SONet achieves sub-second inferences on new problem instances, equating to up to 10,000x speedup over representative baselines. These results suggest that structure-preserving neural operators provide a practical route toward reusable, real-time surrogates for high-dimensional optimal control.

</details>


### [261] [Equilibrium for Time-inconsistent Mean Field Games: A Systematic Analysis by Entropy Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14363)
*Erhan Bayraktar,Zhenhua Wang,Xiang Yu,Keyu Zhang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究连续时间下一般时间不一致平均场博弈问题的均衡存在性与近似。通过引入消失熵正则化方法，将原始非局部均衡HJB系统转化为可解的探索性均衡HJB方程，利用Schauder不动点定理和抛物型正则性估计证明了正则化均衡的全局存在性，并进一步通过紧性论证、Young测度技术和对偶工具证明了当熵正则化趋于零时正则化均衡收敛到原始时间不一致MFG的均衡。此外，还提出了一种策略迭代算法并证明了其在短时间区间和弱终端交互条件下的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决连续时间下一般时间不一致平均场博弈问题中因初始时间依赖性（如非指数贴现）导致的复杂非局部均衡HJB系统的存在性与近似问题。

Method: 采用消失熵正则化方法，将原始均衡HJB系统转化为耦合的探索性均衡HJB方程和依赖于律的随机微分方程；利用Schauder不动点论证和针对值函数与测度流的抛物型正则性估计证明正则化均衡存在性；通过紧性论证、Young测度技术和对偶工具分析正则化趋零时的收敛性；基于熵正则化设计策略迭代算法并分析其收敛性。

Result: 在温和假设下建立了正则化均衡的全局存在性；证明了正则化均衡沿子序列收敛到原始时间不一致MFG的均衡；在短时间区间和弱终端交互条件下证明了策略迭代算法的收敛性。

Conclusion: 熵正则化方法为求解时间不一致MFG提供了一种有效的近似框架，兼具理论上的存在性与收敛性保证以及算法上的可行性。

Abstract: This paper studies the existence and approximation of equilibria for general time-inconsistent mean field game (MFG) problems in the continuous-time setting. To handle the intricate nonlocal equilibrium Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman (EHJB) system arising from initial-time dependence, such as non-exponential discounting, we develop a vanishing entropy regularization approach for solving the MFG. With entropy regularization, we first characterize the regularized equilibrium via a coupled exploratory equilibrium HJB (EEHJB) equation and a law-dependent stochastic differential equation. By exploiting Schauder fixed-point arguments and tailored parabolic regularity estimates in a suitable functional space involving both value functions and measure flows, we establish the global existence of regularized equilibria under mild assumptions. We next analyze convergence as the entropy regularization vanishes. By employing compactness arguments, Young measure techniques, and a duality tool for divergence-form Fokker-Planck equations, we prove that the regularized equilibria converge, up to subsequences, to an equilibrium of the original time-inconsistent MFG. Furthermore, under entropy regularization, we propose a policy iteration algorithm and establish its convergence under a short time horizon and weak terminal interaction conditions.

</details>


### [262] [Boundary null-controllability for the beam equation with classical structural damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14371)
*Sergei Avdonin,Julian Edward*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了区间(0,π)上具有结构阻尼的梁方程在不同边界条件（包括Dirichlet和Neumann控制）下的适定性和零可控性。结果表明：当ρ≤2时，对所有T>0零可控；当ρ>2时，对几乎所有ρ零可控，但对(2,∞)中一个稠密子集上的ρ零可控性失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究结构阻尼梁方程在不同边界控制下的适定性和可控性，特别是阻尼参数ρ对零可控性的影响。

Method: 将边界条件中的f(t)视为控制函数，通过分析不同ρ值下系统的能控性结构，利用泛函分析和偏微分方程理论进行证明。

Result: 1) 对所有ρ≤2，系统零可控；2) 对ρ>2，零可控性对几乎所有ρ成立，但在(2,∞)的一个稠密子集上失败。

Conclusion: 结构阻尼梁方程的零可控性依赖于阻尼参数ρ：小阻尼(ρ≤2)保证可控性，大阻尼(ρ>2)时可控性在拓扑意义下“几乎处处”成立但存在反例稠密集。

Abstract: Let $Δ$ be the Dirichlet Laplacian on the interval $(0,π)$, and let $T>0$. We prove a well-posedness results for the structurally damped beam equation $$u_{tt}+Δ^2 u-ρΔu_t=0, x\in (0,π),t>0$$ with various boundary conditions including $$ u(0,t)=u_{xx}(0,t)=0; u(π,t)=f(t),u_{xx}(π,t)=0, $$ and $f\in H_0^2(0,T)$ and appropriate initial conditions. Viewing $f$ as a control, we prove null controllability for all $ρ\leq 2$. For $ρ>2$, we show null controllability for arbitrary $T>0$ holds for almost all $ρ$, but fails for a dense subset of $(2,\infty)$.

We analyze the cases of separable couplings and general utilities, and represent the value of the game as a compilation of the single player problem and a function solving a non local quasilinear pde in the space of measures. We interpret the findings using elements from indifference valuation and arbitrage free pricing, Finally, when the couplings depend only on the average of peer's wealth, we derive explicit solutions and various regularity results for representative cases.

### [264] [Non--exchangeable mean field games with moderate interactions and common noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14901)
*Mao Fabrice Djete*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有适度局部交互和共同噪声的大规模非可交换种群的平均场博弈，提出了松弛形式的极限平均场博弈，证明了存在性、与有限博弈的渐近等价性，并建立了从近似闭环纳什均衡到松弛解的双向收敛关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有平均场博弈主要针对可交换（交换性）种群，无法刻画实际中普遍存在的异质性局部交互（如图谱型大尺度交互）与共同噪声的耦合效应。

Method: 采用图谱加权局部密度的松弛平均场博弈形式；通过连续性、非退化性和凸性假设证明松弛均衡的存在性及严格化；利用非线性Feynman-Kac表示给出确定性情形下的严格均衡刻画；通过双向渐近分析建立有限博弈与极限模型之间的闭环纳什均衡收敛关系。

Result: 证明了松弛平均场博弈均衡的存在性；在凸性条件下松弛均衡可严格化；无共同噪声时得到确定性均衡及其Feynman-Kac表示；建立了有限博弈近似纳什均衡极限点与松弛解的双向收敛及支付收敛。

Conclusion: 给出了一类非可交换、具有适度局部交互和共同噪声的平均场博弈的完整渐近均衡刻画，为异质性大规模博弈提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study mean field games for large non--exchangeable populations with moderate local interactions and common noise. The finite--player system is driven by two complementary interaction mechanisms : a graphon--type structure, which encodes heterogeneous large--scale interactions between agents, and a rescaled local kernel, which produces a density-dependent interaction term in the limit. The limiting model is a non--exchangeable mean field game in which the representative player is indexed by a label \(u\in[0,1]\), interacts through a graphon--weighted local density, and is affected by a graphon--induced environment law.
  We introduce a relaxed formulation of the limiting mean field game, adapted to the presence of common noise, and prove existence under general continuity and non--degeneracy assumptions. Under additional convexity assumptions, relaxed equilibria can be realized in strict form. In the deterministic case without common noise, we obtain deterministic equilibria and provide a probabilistic characterization of strict equilibria through a nonlinear Feynman--Kac representation.
  We then establish the asymptotic connection with the finite--player game. We prove that every limit point of approximate closed--loop Nash equilibria is a relaxed solution of the limiting mean field game, and that the corresponding averaged equilibrium payoffs converge. Conversely, every relaxed mean field game equilibrium can be approximated by Markovian approximate Nash equilibria of the finite--player systems. These results give a complete asymptotic characterization of equilibrium behavior for non--exchangeable games with moderate interactions and common noise.

### [265] [Scalable Solution of the Stochastic Multi-path Traveling Salesman Problem via Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14662)
*Xiaochen Chou,Ludovica Di Marco,Enza Messina*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 针对多路径随机旅行时间下的旅行商问题，本文提出一种集成神经网络代理模型的两阶段随机规划方法，通过近似第二阶段期望值来提升计算效率与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智慧城市与城市物流中的混合动力车辆路径规划面临多路径随机旅行成本问题，实时交通条件导致旅行时间具有不确定性，传统方法因需要大量场景模拟而计算负担过重，亟需高效求解方法。

Method: 采用两阶段随机规划：第一阶段确定访问位置的顺序（哈密顿回路），第二阶段根据实时交通条件选择最优路径；创新点在于使用神经网络代理模型近似第二阶段期望值，并设计多种网络架构与训练策略。

Result: 初步结果表明，该方法在计算时间、解质量和泛化能力方面均有提升，增强了问题在不确定性下的可扩展性与实际适用性。

Abstract: The multi-path Traveling Salesman Problem with stochastic travel costs arises in hybrid vehicle routing applications designed for Smart City and City Logistics, where multiple paths exist between each pair of locations. Travel times along these paths are typically affected by real-time traffic conditions and therefore modeled as stochastic. The objective of the problem is to determine a Hamiltonian tour that minimizes the expected total travel cost under uncertainty. In this work, we adopt a two-stage stochastic programming formulation. In the first stage, a predefined route specifying the sequence of locations to be visited is determined, while taking into consideration a second-stage recourse problem that selects the optimal path from the feasible set of alternative paths for each pair of locations, once real-time traffic conditions are realized. To reduce the computational burden imposed by the large number of scenarios required to capture travel time uncertainty, the innovation of this work is the integration of neural network-based surrogate models to approximate the expected value of the second-stage recourse problem. Different architectures and training strategies for the neural networks are proposed and analyzed, with performance evaluated in terms of computation time, solution quality, and generalization capability. Preliminary findings demonstrate the enhanced scalability and practical applicability of the approach for complex vehicle routing problems under uncertainty.

### [266] [AIS: Adaptive Importance Sampling for Quantized RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13907)
*Jiajun Zhou,Wei Shao,Lingchao Zheng,Yuwei Fan,Ngai Wong*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 针对LLM强化学习中低精度rollout（FP8）与BF16训练器不匹配导致训练崩溃的问题，提出自适应重要性采样（AIS）框架，通过每批次动态调整干预强度，在保留FP8加速优势的同时恢复BF16基线性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM强化学习被rollout生成的高成本所主导，低精度rollout（FP8）与高精度训练器（BF16）之间的不匹配会引入非平稳偏差，早期虽提供随机探索奖励，后期却导致训练崩溃。

Method: 提出自适应重要性采样（AIS），结合权重可靠性、散度严重性和方差放大三个实时诊断指标，生成混合系数在未校正梯度与完全重要性加权梯度之间插值，抑制不匹配的失稳成分同时保留探索收益。

Result: 在LLaDA-8B-Instruct、Qwen3-8B和Qwen3.5-9B上，AIS在多数任务上匹配BF16基线性能，同时保持FP8带来1.5至2.76倍的rollout加速。

Conclusion: AIS有效解决了低精度rollout与高精度训练器的不匹配问题，在不牺牲训练稳定性的前提下实现了显著的加速收益。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) is dominated by the cost of rollout generation, which has motivated the use of low-precision rollouts (e.g., FP8) paired with a BF16 trainer to improve throughput and reduce memory pressure. This introduces a rollout-training mismatch that biases the policy gradient and can cause training to collapse outright on reasoning benchmarks. We show that the mismatch is non-stationary and acts as a double-edged sword: early in training it provides a stochastic exploration bonus, exposing the gradient to trajectories the trainer would otherwise under-sample, but the same perturbation transitions into a destabilizing source of bias as the policy concentrates.
  To solve this, we propose Adaptive Importance Sampling (AIS), a correction framework that adjusts the strength of its intervention on a per-batch basis. AIS combines three real-time diagnostics, namely weight reliability, divergence severity, and variance amplification, into a single mixing coefficient that interpolates between the uncorrected and fully importance-weighted gradients, suppressing the destabilizing component of the mismatch while preserving its exploratory benefit. We integrate AIS into GRPO and evaluate it on the diffusion-based LLaDA-8B-Instruct and the autoregressive Qwen3-8B and Qwen3.5-9B across mathematical reasoning and planning benchmarks. AIS matches the BF16 baseline on most tasks while retaining the 1.5 to 2.76x rollout speedup of FP8.

*Andrea Schioppa,Tim Salimans*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 利用Tweedie公式估计协方差；2) 对协方差矩阵进行结构化傅里叶空间分解以提高计算效率；3) 作为DDIM的扩展实现，每步仅增加一次Jacobian-向量积(JVP)计算。

Abstract: We present a covariance-aware sampler that improves the quality of pixel-space Diffusion Model (DM) sampling in the few-step regime. We hypothesize that in the few-step regime samplers fail because they rely solely on the predicted mean of the reverse distribution, while our solution explicitly models the reverse-process covariance. Our method combines Tweedie's formula to estimate the covariance with an efficient, structured Fourier-space decomposition of the covariance matrix. Implemented as an extension of DDIM, our method requires only a minimal overhead: one extra Jacobian-Vector Product (JVP) per step. We demonstrate that for pixel-based DMs, our method consistently produces superior samples compared to state-of-the-art second order samplers (Heun, DPM-Solver++) and the recent aDDIM sampler, at an identical number of function evaluations (NFE).

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将近期工作组织为三步：(1) 扩展PAC-Bayesian理论以处理随机、数据依赖的假设集；(2) 利用优化轨迹的几何与拓扑描述符（分形维数、α加权寿命和、正幅度）细化复杂度项；(3) 用稳定性假设替换信息论项。最终将这些贡献统一到一个模板不等式中并进行对比。

Result: 给出了一个统一的模板不等式框架，并对来自多篇论文（arXiv:2404.17442, arXiv:2006.09313, arXiv:2302.02766, arXiv:2407.08723, arXiv:2507.06775）的泛化界进行了头对头比较。

Conclusion: 通过系统化组织三个关键步骤，该综述为理解过参数化深度网络的泛化提供了统一视角，并展示了非平凡泛化界的可行路径。

Abstract: Deep neural networks generalize well despite being heavily overparameterized, in apparent contradiction with classical learning theory based on uniform convergence over fixed hypothesis spaces. Uniform bounds over the entire parameter space are vacuous in this regime, and recent work has shown that non-vacuous guarantees can be recovered by restricting attention to the part of parameter space that the algorithm actually visits. This survey paper organizes this line of work around three steps: extending PAC-Bayesian theory to random, data-dependent hypothesis sets (arXiv:2404.17442); refining the complexity term with geometric and topological descriptors of the optimization trajectory, including fractal dimensions, alpha-weighted lifetime sums, and positive magnitude (arXiv:2006.09313, arXiv:2302.02766, arXiv:2407.08723); and replacing the resulting information-theoretic terms by stability assumptions (arXiv:2507.06775). We unify these contributions around a single template inequality and a head-to-head comparison of the resulting bounds.

### [269] [Multi-Scale Dequant: Eliminating Dequantization Bottleneck via Activation Decomposition for Efficient LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13915)
*Lingchao Zheng,Yuwei Fan,Jun Li,Chengqiu Hu,Qichen Liao,Junyi Fan,Rui Shi,Fangzheng Miao*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出Multi-Scale Dequant (MSD)量化框架，通过将高精度激活分解为多个低精度分量，直接与量化权重相乘，从而消除GEMM关键路径上的反量化操作，在Ascend NPU等解耦计算架构上显著提升LLM推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在解耦计算单元架构（如Ascend NPU）上，反量化操作（将低比特权重转换回高精度）消耗的周期甚至超过矩阵乘法本身，导致高吞吐张量核心利用率不足，成为LLM推理的瓶颈。

Method: MSD将高精度BF16激活分解为多个低精度分量，每个分量直接与量化权重通过原生硬件加速GEMM相乘，避免GEMM前的INT8-to-BF16权重转换。为INT8权重（W4A16）和MXFP4权重（W4A16）分别实例化，并推导了严格误差界。

Result: INT8权重两遍分解达到近16有效比特；MXFP4权重两遍分解达到近6.6有效比特，误差界1/64每块，超越单遍MXFP8（5.24比特）同时保持相同GEMM计算时间。KV缓存HBM流量减少达2.5倍。数值模拟表明不降低精度，且许多设置下L2误差更低。

Conclusion: MSD通过将计算范式从精度转换转为多尺度逼近，有效消除了反量化导致的Vector-Cube流水线停顿，在保持精度的同时显著提升LLM推理效率。

Abstract: Quantization is essential for efficient large language model (LLM) inference, yet the dequantization step-converting low-bit weights back to high-precision for matrix multiplication has become a critical bottleneck on modern AI accelerators. On architectures with decoupled compute units (e.g., Ascend NPUs), dequantization operations can consume more cycles than the matrix multiplication itself, leaving the high-throughput tensor cores underutilized. This paper presents Multi-Scale Dequant (MSD), a quantization framework that removes weight/KV dequantization from the GEMM critical path. Instead of lifting low-bit weights to BF16 precision, MSD decomposes high-precision BF16 activations into multiple low-precision components, each of which can be multiplied directly with quantized weights via native hardware-accelerated GEMM. This approach shifts the computational paradigm from precision conversion to multi-scale approximation, avoiding INT8-to-BF16 weight conversion before GEMM. We instantiate MSD for two weight formats and derive tight error bounds for each. For INT8 weights (W4A16), two-pass INT8 decomposition achieves near 16 effective bits. For MXFP4 weights (W4A16), two-pass MXFP4 decomposition yields near 6.6 effective bits with error bound 1/64 per block surpassing single-pass MXFP8(5.24 bits) while maintaining the same effective GEMM compute time. We further derive closed-form latency and HBM traffic models showing that MSD avoids the Vector-Cube pipeline stall caused by dequantization and reduces KV cache HBM traffic by up to 2.5 times in attention. Numerical simulations on matrix multiplication and Flash Attention kernels confirm that MSD does not degrade accuracy compared to dequantization baselines, and in many settings achieves lower L2 error.

</details>


### [270] [A Regret Perspective on Online Multiple Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13916)
*Qingyang Hao,Kongchang Zhou,Fang Kong,Hongxin Wei*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出加权遗憾（Weighted Regret）作为统一评估在线多重检验（OMT）中假阳性和假阴性不对称代价的指标，并证明遗憾守恒对偶性：严格FDR控制的确定性过程必然遭受Ω(T)线性遗憾惩罚。针对外生测试流，提出Decoupled-OMT（DOMT）元封装器，通过历史解耦的随机扰动缓解阈值枯竭，实现Ω(√T)遗憾降低，并刻画了"冷启动税"相变边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统OMT方法将FDR与统计功效独立评估，忽视了现代自动化流水线中假阳性与假阴性代价的高度不对称性，缺乏统一评估指标。

Method: 提出加权遗憾（Weighted Regret）统一评估指标；证明遗憾守恒对偶性（Duality of Regret Conservation）；提出Decoupled-OMT（DOMT）元封装器，通过历史解耦的非负随机扰动缓解阈值枯竭，在平稳环境下保持精确渐近安全性，在突发环境下实现阶最优的Ω(√T)遗憾降低。

Result: 严格FDR控制的确定性过程必然遭受Ω(T)线性遗憾惩罚；DOMT实现Ω(√T)的阶最优遗憾降低；推导出"冷启动税"（Cold-Start Tax）描述算法优势的精确相变边界；实验验证DOMT持续降低经验加权遗憾，实现阶最优的次线性阈值枯竭缓解。

Conclusion: DOMT作为基线无关的元封装器，通过随机扰动有效缓解确定性OMT过程的阈值枯竭问题，在非平稳Pareto前沿上实现阶最优的加权遗憾权衡。

Abstract: Online Multiple Testing (OMT), a fundamental pillar of sequential statistical inference, traditionally evaluates the False Discovery Rate (FDR) and statistical power in isolation, obscuring the highly asymmetric costs of false positives and false negatives in modern automated pipelines. To unify this evaluation, we introduce $\textit{Weighted Regret}$. Under this metric, we prove the $\textit{Duality of Regret Conservation}$: purely deterministic procedures ensuring strict FDR control inevitably incur an $Ω(T)$ linear regret penalty, as threshold depletion during signal-sparse cold starts forces massive false negatives. Tailored for exogenous testing streams, we propose Decoupled-OMT (DOMT) as a baseline-agnostic meta-wrapper. By incorporating a history-decoupled, strictly non-negative random perturbation, DOMT rescues purely deterministic baselines from severe threshold depletion. Crucially, it preserves exact asymptotic safety in stationary environments and rigorously bounds finite-sample error inflation during cold-starts. Guaranteeing zero additional false negatives, it yields an order-optimal $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret reduction in bursty environments, with a derived ``Cold-Start Tax'' characterizing the exact phase transition of algorithmic superiority. Experiments validate that DOMT consistently curtails empirical weighted regret, achieving an order-optimal sublinear mitigation of threshold depletion to navigate the non-stationary Pareto frontier.

</details>


### [271] [Pause and Reflect: Conformal Aggregation for Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14098)
*Yu Gu,Zijun Yu,Vahid Partovi Nia,Masoud Asgharian*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于共形风险控制的CoT推理方法，通过加权评分聚合替代多数投票，并校准弃权规则，在有限样本下保证置信错误率，无需重新训练即可提升选择性准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在CoT自一致性推理中，正确性不再取决于单条推理路径，而是多条候选路径的聚合规则，导致聚合不确定性成为核心挑战。当错误答案的代价远高于弃权时，需要一种能有效控制置信错误率的方法。

Method: 1) 用加权评分聚合替代多数投票；2) 利用共形风险控制校准弃权规则；3) 识别分数可分性作为弃权提升选择性准确率的关键条件；4) 推导闭合表达式，仅凭校准数据即可预测准确率提升；5) 纯推理时方法，无需重新训练。

Result: 在四个基准、四个开源模型和三类评分上，实际置信错误率与预设目标一致；在GSM8K上，通过弃权不到5%的问题实现90.1%的选择性准确率，相比多数投票基线82%有显著提升。

Conclusion: 该方法有效控制了CoT推理中的聚合不确定性，通过共形预测框架提供了统计保证，并在多个设置下验证了有效性。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning with self-consistency improves performance by aggregating multiple sampled reasoning paths. In this setting, correctness is no longer tied to a single reasoning trace but to the aggregation rule over a pool of candidate paths, making aggregation uncertainty the central challenge. This issue is critical where confidently incorrect answers are far more costly than abstentions. We introduce a conformal procedure for CoT reasoning that directly addresses aggregation uncertainty. Our approach replaces majority voting with weighted score aggregation over reasoning paths and calibrates an abstention rule using conformal risk control. This approach leads to finite-sample guarantees on the confident-error rate--the probability that the system answers and is wrong. We further identify score separability as the key condition under which abstention provably improves selective accuracy, and derive closed-form expressions that predict accuracy gains from calibration data alone. The method is fully inference-time, and requires no retraining. Across four benchmarks, four open-source models, and three score classes, realized confident-error rates are consistent with the prescribed targets up to calibration-split and test-set variability. Our method achieves $90.1\%$ selective accuracy on GSM8K by abstaining on less than $5\%$ of problems, compared with $82\%$ accuracy under majority-voting baseline.

Abstract: Integration against a probability distribution given its unnormalized density is a central task in Bayesian inference and other fields. We introduce new methods for approximating such expectations with a small set of weighted samples -- i.e., a quadrature rule -- constructed via an interacting particle system that minimizes maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) to the target distribution. These methods extend the classical mean shift algorithm, as well as recent algorithms for optimal quantization of empirical distributions, to the case of continuous distributions. Crucially, our approach creates dynamics for MMD minimization that are invariant to the unknown normalizing constant; they also admit both gradient-free and gradient-informed implementations. The resulting mean shift interacting particle systems converge quickly, capture anisotropy and multi-modality, avoid mode collapse, and scale to high dimensions. We demonstrate their performance on a wide range of benchmark sampling problems, including multi-modal mixtures, Bayesian hierarchical models, PDE-constrained inverse problems, and beyond.

### [273] [On the Burden of Achieving Fairness in Conformal Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14260)

Motivation: 保形预测常用单一 pooled 阈值进行校准，但这种方法可能掩盖不同群体之间分数分布的异质性，导致组间覆盖率失真。作者希望从群体分布的角度系统研究这一现象，并为公平导向的校准选择提供理论依据。

Result: (1) 推导了守恒定律和下界，证明 pooled 校准会以组间分位数异质性的尺度引入不可约的覆盖率扭曲；(2) 证明 Equalized Coverage 和 Equalized Set Size 两种公平定义存在根本性矛盾；(3) 量化了按组处理与 pooled 处理之间的双向权衡代价；(4) 实验证实了覆盖率与集合大小维度之间的双向权衡。

Abstract: Conformal prediction is often calibrated with a single pooled threshold, but this can hide cross-group heterogeneity in score distributions and distort group-wise coverage. We study this phenomenon through the population score distributions underlying split conformal calibration. First, we derive a conservation law and lower bound showing that pooled calibration incurs irreducible group-wise coverage distortion at a scale set by cross-group quantile heterogeneity. Second, we demonstrate that the two leading fairness definitions for conformal prediction, Equalized Coverage and Equalized Set Size, are fundamentally in tension. Third, we quantify the cost of moving between policies which treat groups separately or pool them. Experiments on synthetic and real data confirm the same bidirectional trade-off after finite-sample calibration. Our results show that, for the policy families studied here, calibration choice does not remove cross-group heterogeneity; it determines whether the resulting distortion appears in the coverage or size dimension, providing a principled lens for analyzing fairness-oriented calibration choices in practice.

Abstract: Diffusion models generate samples by denoising along the score of a perturbed target distribution. In practice, one trains a neural diffusion model, which is computationally expensive. Recent work suggests that score matching implicitly smooths the empirical score, and that this smoothing bias promotes generalization by capturing low-dimensional data geometry. We propose moment-matched score-smoothed overdamped Langevin dynamics (MM-SOLD), a training-free interacting particle sampler that enforces the target moments throughout the sampling trajectory. We prove that, in the large-particle limit, the empirical particle density converges to a deterministic limit whose one-particle stationary marginal is a Gibbs--Boltzmann density obtained by exponentially tilting a naive score-smoothed diffusion target. The mean and covariance of this distribution agree with the empirical moments of the training data. ### [277] [Average Gradient Outer Product in kernel regression provably recovers the central subspace for multi-index models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15082)
*Libin Zhu,Damek Davis,Dmitriy Drusvyatskiy,Maryam Fazel*

Main category: stat.ML

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究学习器在样本数量不足以实现准确预测时，是否仍能发现数据中有效的低维结构，并解释迭代核方法（如RFM）在实践中的样本效率。

Result: 当目标函数f*的阶数为p*时，KRR需要n≍d^{p*}样本才能准确预测；但如果f*的低阶p成分已包含所有相关方向，子空间恢复仅需n≍d^{p+δ}样本（δ∈(0,1)），实现了预测与表征的分离。

Abstract: We study a prototypical situation when a learned predictor can discover useful low-dimensional structure in data, while using fewer samples than are needed for accurate prediction. Specifically, we consider the problem of recovering a multi-index polynomial $f^*(x)=h(Ux)$, with $U\in\mathbb{R}^{r\times d}$ and $r\ll d$, from finitely many data/label pairs. Importantly, the target function depends on input $x$ only through the projection onto an unknown $r$-dimensional central subspace. The algorithm we analyze is appealingly simple: fit kernel ridge regression (KRR) to the data and compute the Average Gradient Outer Product (AGOP) from the fitted predictor. Our main results show that under reasonable assumptions the top $r$-dimensional eigenspace of AGOP provably recovers the central subspace, even in regimes when the prediction error remains large. Specifically, if the target function $f^*$ has degree $p^*$, it is known that $n\asymp d^{p^*}$ samples are necessary for KRR to achieve accurate prediction. In contrast, we show that if a low degree $p$ component of $f^*$ already carries all relevant directions for prediction, subspace recovery occurs in the much lower sample regime $n\asymp d^{p+δ}$ for any $δ\in(0,1)$. Our results thus demonstrate a separation between prediction and representation, and provide an explanation for why iterative kernel methods such as Recursive Feature Machines (RFM) can be sample-efficient in practice.

*Lanxin Xiang,Liang Shi,Youhui Ye,Boyu Jiang,Dawei Zhou,Feng Guo*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出RoSHAP框架，通过自助重采样和核密度估计建模SHAP值的分布，解决特征归因中的随机波动问题。RoSHAP指标同时奖励活跃、强健和稳定的特征，在模拟和真实实验中优于单次归因方法，且用更少特征达到全特征模型的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 特征归因分析在解释机器学习模型中至关重要，但现有归因度量存在随机波动问题：不同训练-测试划分、随机种子或模型拟合过程会产生显著不同的归因值和特征排序，导致解释结果不可靠。

Method: 提出RoSHAP框架：1) 通过自助重采样（bootstrap resampling）和核密度估计（kernel density estimation）建模特征归因得分的分布；2) 在温和正则条件下证明聚合后的特征归因得分渐近服从高斯分布，从而大幅降低分布估计的计算成本；3) RoSHAP指标通过汇总SHAP分布，同时奖励活跃性（active）、强度（strong）和稳定性（stable）的特征。

Result: 模拟和真实数据实验表明：RoSHAP框架在识别信号特征方面优于标准的单次归因度量；使用RoSHAP筛选特征构建的模型，其预测性能与全特征模型相当，但使用的预测因子大幅减少。

Conclusion: RoSHAP方法提升了机器学习模型的稳定性和可解释性，能够为数据分析提供可靠且一致的洞见。

Abstract: Feature attribution analysis is critical for interpreting machine learning models and supporting reliable data-driven decisions. However, feature attribution measures often exhibit stochastic variation: different train--test splits, random seeds, or model-fitting procedures can produce substantially different attribution values and feature rankings. This paper proposes a framework for incorporating stochastic nature of feature attribution and a robust attribution metric, RoSHAP, for stable feature ranking based on the SHAP metric. The proposed framework models the distribution of feature attribution scores and estimates it through bootstrap resampling and kernel density estimation. We show that, under mild regularity conditions, the aggregated feature attribution score is asymptotically Gaussian, which greatly reduces the computational cost of distribution estimation. The RoSHAP summarizes the distribution of SHAP into a robust feature-ranking criterion that simultaneously rewards features that are active, strong, and stable. Through simulations and real-data experiments, the proposed framework and RoSHAP outperform standard single-run attribution measures in identifying signal features. In addition, models built using RoSHAP-selected features achieve predictive performance comparable to full-feature models while using substantially fewer predictors. The proposed RoSHAP approach improves the stability and interpretability of machine learning models, enabling reliable and consistent insights for analysis.

</details>
